# Context Mode Index

Index local project content for later search.

## Instructions

1. Prefer the `ctx_index` MCP tool when it is available.
2. Ask for a path only if the user did not provide one and the current project root is ambiguous.
3. Use `path`, not large inline `content`, so file bytes do not enter the conversation.
4. For repository indexing, pass conservative bounds and a clear source label:

```javascript
ctx_index({
  path: ".",
  source: "project:<name>",
  maxDepth: 5,
  maxFiles: 200
})
```

5. If MCP tools are unavailable, fall back to the CLI:

```bash
context-mode index . --source project:<name>
```

6. Report the indexed source label, file count or section count, and the matching search command:

```javascript
ctx_search({ source: "project:<name>", queries: ["..."] })
```

## Safety

- Do not index dependency directories, build outputs, secrets, or generated artifacts.
- Prefer `--exclude` or `exclude` for project-specific noisy paths.
- For broad repos, ask the user before raising `maxFiles` above 500.

# Existing Test Harness Map — `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`

## 0. Top-level layout

- Program under test: `/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails` — a single **extension-less** executable Python file (not a package/module).
- Test wrapper: `/workspace/run-tests` (executable Python).
- Config: `/workspace/pyproject.toml` (`[tool.pytest.ini_options]`, `[tool.coverage.run]`).
- Tests root: `/workspace/tests/`.
- Design docs: `/workspace/development/2026-07-04-test-harness/SPEC.md`, `/workspace/tests/README.md`.
- Maintenance prompt templates: `/workspace/prompts/add-tests-for-change.prompt.md`, `/workspace/prompts/refresh-fixtures.prompt.md` (referenced by SPEC §8).

---

## 1. SPEC.md summary (`/workspace/development/2026-07-04-test-harness/SPEC.md`)

**Approach chosen: "C — Hybrid" (§4).** One tiny behavior-preserving source change makes the program importable; then three interception styles coexist: monkeypatch (unit/integration), a PATH-shim fake `terminus` (e2e), and real read-only Terminus (live, the default).

**Architecture (§5):**

- **§5.0 Frameworks:** pytest (spine) + syrupy (golden snapshots) + Hypothesis (property) + pytest-cov (measured, **no gate**) + pytest-playwright (render, manages its own Chromium). No PHP test framework — `inline-styles.php` is exercised as a subprocess file-in/file-out transform.
- **§5.1 The seam (only source change):** wrap the old inline ~77-line argparse block into `build_arg_parser()` + `parse_args(argv=None)`, and only call `parse_args()` from the `__main__` block, so import has no argv side effects. "Behavior-preserving" is pinned by a byte-identity gate (acceptance #10).
- **§5.2 Global-state isolation:** `script_context.py` holds process-global mutable state. An autouse fixture **deep-copies** and restores 8 attrs per test (`sc.hooks` is a dict-of-lists mutated in place by `add_hook`/`add_notice`/`add_news_item`, so shallow copy would leak).
- **§5.4 Tiers/marks:** `unit`, `integration`, `e2e`, `live`, `render`, `email`, `slow`. **Live is the default** (`./run-tests` runs it); `--fast` selects `-m "not live and not slow"` for the hermetic offline inner loop.
- **§5.5 Mock seams (both styles):** monkeypatch `run_terminus`/`terminus` on the loaded module returning `(stdout, stderr, fatal)`; PATH-shim fake `terminus` for full e2e; live = no interception. `run_terminus` is the primary seam (all Pantheon/WP/Drush I/O funnels through it).
- **§5.6 DB:** temp sqlite fixtures, schema created via `Base.metadata.create_all`; repo DB never touched.
- **§5.7 Config:** self-contained `fixtures/config/minimal.toml`, `full.toml`; NEVER depend on the private production config symlink.
- **§5.8 `run-tests` wrapper** — flag table (see §3 below).
- **§5.9 Golden normalization:** volatile `make_msgid` CIDs → `cid:NORMALIZED`; `--date` pinned; `.txt` already deterministic.
- **§5.10 Property scope:** Hypothesis on pure functions (`fix_drush_output`, `escape_url`, traffic aggregation). The **plan-recommendation cost model is inline in `main()` (~lines 3095-3211)** and not directly callable — pinned via parametrized e2e for now; a `recommend_plan(...)` extraction is deferred (pulls in `plan_info`, current plan, `PantheonOverageProtection` lookups, overage block size/cost, estimate, `site_plan_start`).
- **§5.11 Safety interlock (Prime Directive #1):** `run_program()` is the ONLY sanctioned invocation path; before exec it raises **`ForbiddenFlagError`** (named exception, not bare assert/silent skip) if `--all`/`-a`/`--for-real` appear. Covered by its own test.

**§3.1 two confirmed bugs fixed with the harness (each has a regression):**
1. `terminus()` session-expiry retry (~`:320-337`) did `del args["pshe-no-retry"]` / `args.push(...)` on a `*args` **tuple** → TypeError/AttributeError; crashed instead of retrying on `Invalid or expired session header`.
2. `check/umich/__init__.py:11` else branch called `sc.console('…')` (a rich `Console` instance) as a callable → TypeError; should be `sc.console.print(…)`.
Plus two non-UMich render-path bugs (`contacts` UnboundLocalError; unconditional `if True:` UMich annual-billing block) regressed by the offline e2e.

**§9 smoke-per-tier table**, **§11 GMail email tier** (scaffolded + skipped, C4), **§13 acceptance criteria**, **§14 explicitly out of scope** (full suite, SMTP/SendGrid, big refactor, CI, coverage gaps accepted by C1–C4: the `--all` aggregation/CSV path and real send path are untested by design).

---

## 2. `tests/` directory — file by file

### `tests/conftest.py` (`/workspace/tests/conftest.py`, 354 lines)
The heart of the harness. Key contents:

- **Constants:** `REPO_ROOT`, `PROGRAM` (= repo root / `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`), `SHIM_DIR` (`tests/shims`), `TERMINUS_FIXTURES` (`tests/fixtures/terminus`), `CONFIG_DIR`, `REAL_TERMINUS` (from env `TERMINUS_SHIM_REAL`, default `/usr/local/bin/terminus`).
- **MPLBACKEND=Agg** set at conftest import time (line 31: `os.environ.setdefault("MPLBACKEND", "Agg")`) — must precede the target module because it imports `matplotlib.pyplot` at top level.
- **Exceptions:** `ForbiddenFlagError(RuntimeError)`, `FixtureNotFoundError(FileNotFoundError)`.
- **psh loader** (`_load_main_module` + session-scoped `psh` fixture, lines 67-81):
  ```python
  loader = SourceFileLoader("psh_main", str(PROGRAM))
  spec = importlib.util.spec_from_loader("psh_main", loader)
  module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
  loader.exec_module(module)
  ```
  Cached in module global `_main_module` so SQLAlchemy models are registered only once.
- **`reset_sc` (autouse fixture, lines 97-121):** `import script_context as sc`; deep-copies `_SC_ATTRS = (options, config, news, hooks, substitutions, plugin, check, plugin_context)`, sets a clean slate (`sc.options = psh.parse_args([])`, `sc.hooks = {"setup": [], "check": []}`, etc.), yields `sc`, and restores saved values in `finally`.
- **`temp_db` fixture + `TempDB` class (lines 125-143):** builds `psh.db.create_engine(f"sqlite:///{path}")`, `psh.Base.metadata.create_all(...)`, `sessionmaker`, exposes `PantheonTraffic` / `PantheonOverageProtection`. Uses `tmp_path`; disposes engine on teardown.
- **`make_workdir` (147-160):** temp CWD, symlinks repo assets `_CWD_ASSETS = ("email_template.html", "email_template.txt", "header-image.png", "inline-styles.php")`, empty `news/`, neutral `fqdns.json = "{}"` (offline-safe — DNS loop finds nothing).
- **Golden normalization (175-180):** `_CID_RE = re.compile(r"cid:[^\"'\s&gt;]+")`; `normalize_report_html()` → `cid:NORMALIZED`.
- **`seed_traffic` (183-200):** inserts a deterministic month of `pantheon_traffic` rows via raw sqlite3 (`visits = 1000 + day.day*10`, pages = visits*3, cache = visits*2).
- **E2E constants (168-172):** `E2E_SITE="its-wws-test1"`, `E2E_SITE_ID="9cf2c790-c7b8-4f2f-a6f1-27385b8f958e"`, `E2E_DATE="2026-03-31"` (March avoids the June contract-year-end U-M-only path), `E2E_SMTP_USERNAME="testuser"`, `MINIMAL_CONFIG`.
- **`build_rendered_report` (203-227):** runs `--create-tables` (exits non-zero by design via `sys.exit("Tables created.")`), asserts `test.db` exists, seeds traffic, then runs `[E2E_SITE, --date, --smtp-username, --config]` — all through `run_program`.
- **`rendered_report` (session-scoped fixture, 230-244):** runs the offline pipeline once; returns dict with `work`, `proc`, `build`, `html`, `txt`, `eml`, `inline2` paths.
- **Safety interlock (247-307):**
  - `FORBIDDEN_FLAGS = {"--all", "-a", "--for-real"}`, `_FORBIDDEN_LONG = ("--all", "--for-real")`.
  - `_assert_flags_allowed(args)` — fail-closed, checks THREE forms: exact token (splitting on `=`), argparse **abbreviation** prefixes (`--fo`→`--for-real`, `--al`→`--all`), and bundled short flags containing `a` (`-av`). Stops at `--`.
  - `run_program(args, *, cwd, mode="replay", extra_env=None, timeout=300)` — stringifies args, calls `_assert_flags_allowed`, then sets env: prepends `SHIM_DIR` to `PATH`, `TERMINUS_SHIM_DIR`, `TERMINUS_SHIM_MODE`, `TERMINUS_SHIM_REAL`, `MPLBACKEND=Agg`; `subprocess.run(..., capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=...)`.
- **Fixtures exposing internals:** `program_runner` (→ `run_program`), `forbidden_flag_error` (→ the class object, deliberately to avoid the conftest double-import identity trap), `normalize_html` (→ `normalize_report_html`).
- **`--llm` reporting (330-353):** `pytest_addoption` adds `--llm`; `pytest_terminal_summary` emits `LLM_SUMMARY passed=… failed=… error=… skipped=… xfailed=… xpassed=…` plus `FAILED &lt;nodeid&gt;` lines.

### `tests/shims/terminus` (`/workspace/tests/shims/terminus`, 91 lines)
Fake `terminus` executable placed on PATH by `run_program`.
- **Record/replay keying:** `_IGNORED_FLAGS = {"--no-ansi", "--no-interaction"}` stripped; `_key(argv)` = `sha1(json.dumps(_key_args(argv)))[:16]` → `&lt;hash&gt;.json` filename.
- **`replay` mode (default):** looks up `TERMINUS_SHIM_DIR/&lt;key&gt;.json`, prints recorded stdout/stderr, exits recorded code. **Missing fixture = LOUD failure: exit 3 + stderr `terminus-shim: no fixture for: …`** (never silent empty).
- **`record` mode:** runs real terminus (`TERMINUS_SHIM_REAL`), tees output, writes JSON `{argv, full_argv, returncode, stdout, stderr, recorded}`.
- Missing `TERMINUS_SHIM_DIR` → exit 2.

### `tests/tools/record.py` (`/workspace/tests/tools/record.py`, 99 lines)
Invoked by `./run-tests --record`. Imports `tests/conftest.py` (single source of truth for constants + `run_program`/`make_workdir`). Runs `--create-tables` then a LIVE read-only run of `its-wws-test1` with shim in `record` mode, then **`scrub()`**:
- `org:site:list` → keep only the test site (asserts exactly 1).
- `domain:list` → keep only `type=="platform"` (drops custom domains so replay makes no live DNS calls).
- `site:team:list` → replace real member emails with `test-owner{1,2}@umich.edu`.
Each rewritten fixture gets a `_scrubbed` note. Never uses `--all`/`--for-real`.

### `tests/fixtures/`
- `config/minimal.toml` — self-contained; all plugins disabled (Cloudflare/AWS `enabled=false`, no `[UMich]` section), relative DB (`test.db`) + News (`./news`) paths, full `[Pantheon.plan_info.*]` / `plan_sku_to_name` tables, non-secret `org_id`.
- `config/full.toml` — the richer config (for deferred SiteLens-gauge/umich paths).
- `terminus/*.json` — 11 recorded fixtures keyed by argv sha1 (e.g. `22d62f1ca472b67c.json` = `wp … eval "echo $wp_version"`). Each carries `argv`, `full_argv`, `returncode`, `stdout`, `stderr`, `recorded`.

### `tests/__snapshots__` → actually `tests/e2e/__snapshots__/test_golden.ambr`
syrupy AMBR golden. Contains `test_rendered_html_matches_golden` (normalized HTML, ~665 lines) and `test_rendered_txt_matches_golden`. Title line shows the pinned date: `… Mar 31, 2026`.

### Existing test files (marks + idioms)

| File | Mark(s) | What it tests / idioms |
|---|---|---|
| `tests/unit/test_pure_functions.py` | `pytestmark = pytest.mark.unit` | `psh.escape_url`, `psh.fix_drush_output` — pure I/O-free; calls functions as `psh.&lt;fn&gt;`; relies on autouse `reset_sc` for `sc.options`. |
| `tests/unit/test_interlock.py` | `unit` | Parametrized `["--all","-a","--for-real","--al","--fo","--for","-av","-va"]` → `pytest.raises(forbidden_flag_error)` via `program_runner`. Also asserts `--help` does NOT raise. |
| `tests/unit/test_property.py` | `unit` | Hypothesis `@given(st.text())` over `fix_drush_output` — type invariants, idempotence, leading-noise-moved-to-errors. |
| `tests/integration/test_terminus_seam.py` | `integration` | `monkeypatch.setattr(psh, "run_terminus", lambda *a,**k: (...))`; `psh.terminus(...)`; `temp_db` round-trip; `sc.add_hook("check", …)` + `sc.invoke_hooks("check", ctx)`. Imports `from conftest import E2E_SITE_ID`. |
| `tests/integration/test_regressions.py` | `integration` | The two §3.1 bug regressions. Monkeypatches `run_terminus` AND `psh.time.sleep`; asserts retry count == 2. Loads `check/umich/__init__.py` via its own `SourceFileLoader`. |
| `tests/e2e/test_shim_e2e.py` | `e2e` | Consumes `rendered_report`; asserts artifacts exist/non-empty, HTML content, dev-mode `To: testuser@umich.edu`. |
| `tests/e2e/test_golden.py` | `e2e` | `assert normalize_html(html) == snapshot` and raw `.txt == snapshot` (syrupy `snapshot` fixture). |
| `tests/render/test_render.py` | `render` | Extracts `cid:` images from `.eml`, rewrites to `file://` URIs, `sync_playwright()`; **skips** (not fails) if Chromium can't launch with hint `python -m playwright install --with-deps chromium`. Asserts title + `img.banner_image` count + `naturalWidth&gt;0`. |
| `tests/live/test_live_smoke.py` | `[live, slow]` | Real `psh.terminus("self:info")` and `site:info its-wws-test1` — no shim on PATH in-process. |
| `tests/email/test_email_roundtrip.py` | `email` | Single `@pytest.mark.skip(reason="email send is disabled until SMTP/SendGrid lands (SPEC §11, C4)")` test documenting the future 5-step GMail flow. |

### Helpers/utilities in `tests/`
- `tests/tools/record.py` (above).
- `tests/conftest.py` module-level functions reused by tests and tooling: `make_workdir`, `seed_traffic`, `build_rendered_report`, `normalize_report_html`, and the constants (`E2E_SITE_ID` imported directly in integration tests).
- `tests/README.md` — dev-facing docs (layout, marks, how to write a test per tier, recording/normalization).

---

## 3. `run-tests` wrapper (`/workspace/run-tests`, 50 lines)

Thin Python over `python -m pytest`. `wrapper_flags = {--fast, --llm, --human, --coverage, --update-goldens, --record}`; everything else is passthrough (`-k`, `-m`, paths). Base args always include `-p no:cacheprovider`.

| Flag | Maps to |
|---|---|
| (none) | default rich output, **all tiers incl. live** |
| `--record` | shells out to `tests/tools/record.py` and returns (short-circuits pytest) |
| `--fast` | `-m "not live and not slow"` (hermetic offline subset) |
| `--llm` | `--llm -q --tb=short --color=no --no-header` (plus the conftest `LLM_SUMMARY`/`FAILED` hook) |
| `--coverage` | `--cov --cov-report=term-missing` (no gate) |
| `--update-goldens` | `--snapshot-update` (syrupy) |

Tiers → marks selection is done purely through pytest `-m` expressions; Claude Code narrows per-change with `-k` (e.g. `-k drupal`).

---

## 4. pytest / coverage config (`/workspace/pyproject.toml`)

- `[project.optional-dependencies] test = ["pytest", "syrupy", "hypothesis", "pytest-cov", "pytest-playwright"]`.
- `[tool.pytest.ini_options]`: `testpaths = ["tests"]`; **no `addopts`** (flags come from `run-tests`); registered `markers`: `unit`, `integration`, `e2e`, `live`, `render`, `email`, `slow` (each with a description string).
- `[tool.coverage.run]`: `include = ["*/pantheon-sitehealth-emails"]` (an **include glob, not `source`**, because the target is a single extension-less file). Measures in-process tiers only unless `COVERAGE_PROCESS_START` plumbing is wired (not present).
- `[tool.setuptools] py-modules = []` (so setuptools doesn't try to package the extension-less file).

---

## 5. The `build_arg_parser()`/`parse_args()` seam and how tests set `sc.options`

In `/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails`:
- Lines 145-226: `def build_arg_parser() -&gt; argparse.ArgumentParser:` builds the parser with **`allow_abbrev=False`** (rejects `--for`→`--for-real`, `--al`→`--all` as a safety guard — note the conftest interlock still defends against abbreviations independently). Positional `sites` (`nargs="*"`), plus `--all/-a`, `--date/-d`, `--update`, `--for-real`, `--config/-c`, `--only-warn`, `--smtp-username/-u`, `--create-tables`, `--import-older-metrics`, `--verbose/-v` (count).
- Lines 229-230: `def parse_args(argv=None): return build_arg_parser().parse_args(argv)`.
- `parse_args(sys.argv)` is only invoked from the `__main__` block, so `import` has zero argv side effects (the whole point of the §5.1 seam). Every function reads `sc.options` at call time.

**How tests populate `sc.options`:** the autouse `reset_sc` fixture sets `sc.options = psh.parse_args([])` — a real parsed default `Namespace` (critical because many helpers call `sc.debug()` → `sc.options.verbose`). Tests that need specific options mutate the namespace directly (e.g. `sc.config = {...}` in `test_regressions.py`), and full-pipeline behavior is exercised by passing real argv lists to `run_program(...)`, which runs the program as a subprocess where its own `__main__`/`parse_args(sys.argv)` builds `sc.options`.

# Supporting context for the `pantheon-sitehealth-emails` test suite

## 1. `prompts/` directory

Four files (`/workspace/prompts/`):

### `/workspace/prompts/add-tests-for-change.prompt.md`
A reusable prompt for adding tests after a code change. Establishes the tier-selection convention and hard safety rules:
- Tier routing by what changed: pure/in-process logic → `tests/unit/` (add a **Hypothesis property test** if the function is pure with an invariant); anything through `run_terminus`/WP/Drush/DB/check-hook → `tests/integration/` (monkeypatch `run_terminus`, use `temp_db`); rendered-report/pipeline changes → extend `e2e` + the `golden` snapshot (add a `live` case if real Pantheon interaction changes); rendering/CSS/template changes → the `render` tier.
- Reuse existing fixtures: `psh`, `reset_sc`, `temp_db`, `program_runner`, `rendered_report`, `minimal_config`. "Never invoke the program except via `run_program` (the `--all`/`--for-real` interlock)."
- Refresh fixtures with `./run-tests --record`; refresh snapshots with `./run-tests --update-goldens`; then `./run-tests --fast` must be green.
- Convention: "Keep any institution-specific logic behind config flags / the `umich` plugin+check packages so the non-UMich path keeps working."
- References `tests/README.md` and `development/2026-07-04-test-harness/SPEC.md` as the authority.

### `/workspace/prompts/refresh-fixtures.prompt.md`
Prompt to refresh recorded Terminus fixtures and golden snapshots. Workflow:
1. `./run-tests --record` — runs live read-only against **`its-wws-test1`**, re-captures Terminus responses, re-applies trims/scrubs (org list → test site only, domain list → platform domain only, team emails → `test-owner{1,2}@umich.edu`).
2. `git diff tests/fixtures/terminus/` — verify no real customer data/emails leaked, only expected fields moved, each fixture keeps a `recorded` date.
3. `./run-tests --fast`; if rendered output changed intentionally, `./run-tests --update-goldens`.
4. Run `live` tier (`./run-tests -m live`) to confirm real Terminus surface still matches fixtures.
- Convention/safety: never commit fixtures with real owner emails or the full org site list; the scrub/trim lives in **`tests/tools/record.py`**.

### `/workspace/prompts/new-feature-design.prompt-template.md`
An 11-KB design-only meta-prompt (persona: "senior software architect with 12 years experience"). It does NOT implement — it produces a `SPEC.md` in the prompt's own directory. Key sections and their conventions:
- **Task**: may split into numbered sub-tasks with a `00-overview.md` index (state, cross-cutting conventions, dependencies, hand-off record). Design only.
- **Methodology**: generate/evaluate multiple solutions, score them, write `SPEC.md` optimized for Claude Code. SPEC must include: which tests to write (all appropriate types — e2e, integration, unit, property), that it must **"reuse the existing harness and honor its hard safety constraints — do not invent a parallel testing approach"**, concrete verifiable acceptance criteria (exact commands + observable outcomes, including test/lint/format runs), README/CLAUDE.md updates, and new end-user docs in `./docs` (docs are end-user only, "not internal functioning").
- **Prime Directives**, **Engineering Preferences** (DRY; "well-tested code is non-negotiable, I'd rather have too many tests than too few"; observability/security not optional; feature flags for non-atomic deploys), **Quality control** (refine until each dimension ≥ 0.9), **Adversarial Review** (dispatch an independent reviewer subagent, 5 dimensions — Completeness/Consistency/Clarity/Scope/Feasibility — max 3 iterations, convergence guard writes "Reviewer Concerns" into the doc).

### `/workspace/prompts/update-claude-md.md`
Prompt for maintaining CLAUDE.md. Convention: "Keep CLAUDE.md focused on things that you can't easily learn by looking at the code," plus anything needed to prevent future-session mistakes.

---

## 2. `plugin/` directory

`/workspace/plugin/__init__.py` and `/workspace/plugin/aws/__init__.py`… note **`plugin/__init__.py`, `plugin/aws/__init__.py` are empty at top / the package `__init__` does the registration**. All packages import `script_context as sc` and self-register at import time behind a config guard. Registration goes through `sc.substitutions.append(...)` (template `$`-substitution functions) and/or `sc.add_hook(...)` / `sc.hooks[...].append(...)`.

### `plugin/aws` (`/workspace/plugin/aws/__init__.py`, `/workspace/plugin/aws/get_secret.py`)
- **Config guard**: `if 'AWS' in sc.config and 'enabled' in sc.config['AWS'] and sc.config['AWS']['enabled']:`
- **On enable**: sets `AWS_PROFILE` / `AWS_DEFAULT_REGION` env vars from config if not already set, then registers a **substitution** `['secret', 'aws', '$name', '$key'] → get_secret($name, $key)`.
- **External I/O** (`get_secret.py`): uses **boto3** `Session().client('secretsmanager').get_secret_value(SecretId=...)`; decodes `SecretString` or base64 `SecretBinary`, `json.loads`, caches in a module-level `secrets` dict. Deliberately does not catch AWS exceptions. Raises `KeyError` for missing key. Test candidate: pure caching/parse logic around a mockable boto client (`botocore.stub`/moto).

### `plugin/cloudflare` (`/workspace/plugin/cloudflare/__init__.py`, `/workspace/plugin/cloudflare/ips.py`)
- **Config guard**: `if 'Cloudflare' in sc.config and ... sc.config['Cloudflare']['enabled']:`
- **On enable**: overrides `member_email`/`member_api_key` from env `CLOUDFLARE_EMAIL`/`CLOUDFLARE_API_KEY`; creates `sc.plugin_context['plugin.cloudflare'] = {}`; registers a **`setup` hook** `plugin.cloudflare.ips.get_cloudflare_ips`.
- **External I/O** (`ips.py`): `from cloudflare import Cloudflare`; `cloudflare.ips.list()` inside `sc.console.status(...)`. On failure `sys.exit('ERROR: Unable to get lists of Cloudflare IPs...')`. Stores parsed `ipaddress.ip_network()` lists into `sc.plugin_context['plugin.cloudflare']['cloudflare_ipv4_nets'/'cloudflare_ipv6_nets']`. Accessors `get_cloudflare_ipv4_nets()`/`get_cloudflare_ipv6_nets()` (note: these read module globals that `get_cloudflare_ips` writes via `global`). Test candidate: mock the `Cloudflare` client, assert CIDR→ip_network conversion and the sys.exit-on-error path.

### `plugin/umich` (`/workspace/plugin/umich/__init__.py`, `/workspace/plugin/umich/portal.py`)
- **Config guard**: `if 'UMich' in sc.config and ... sc.config['UMich']['enabled']:`
- **On enable**: registers a **`setup` hook** `plugin.umich.portal.setup_portal_db`, plus a **substitution** `['umich','portal','plan_info','$plan','$field'] → plan_info($plan,$field)`.
- **External I/O** (`portal.py`): SQLAlchemy engine `mysql+mysqldb://user:pass@host:port/name` from `sc.config['UMich']['portal']['db']` (`echo` on when verbose≥2). Reads tables `sites_site` (→ `portal_sites` keyed by `site_slug`, capturing `id/owner_group/shortcode`) and `sites_pantheonplan` (active plans → `portal_plan_info` traffic_limit/cost, and populates `sc.config['Pantheon']['plan_sku_to_name'][pantheon_plan_sku] = portal_plan_name`). Fires nested hook `sc.invoke_hooks('setup.umich.portal', connection)`, then stores `sc.config['UMich']['portal']['sites']`. So the UMich plugin **dynamically overrides the config's `plan_sku_to_name`** from the portal DB. Test candidate: integration test with a temp MySQL/SQLite-backed engine or mocked connection.

---

## 3. `check/` directory

`/workspace/check/__init__.py` (empty), `/workspace/check/umich/__init__.py`, `/workspace/check/umich/sitelens.py`.

### `/workspace/check/umich/__init__.py`
- Same guard `sc.config['UMich']['enabled']`. If enabled, registers three hooks:
  - `sc.add_hook('setup.umich.portal', {... setup_sitelens})` — nested hook fired by the umich portal plugin (dependency ordering: SiteLens setup runs during the portal DB connection).
  - `sc.add_hook('check', {... check_sitelens_urls})`
  - `sc.add_hook('check', {... check_sitelens_scores})`
- Else prints `Skipping check.umich.sitelens because UMich plugin is not enabled`.

### `/workspace/check/umich/sitelens.py`
- **External data**: `setup_sitelens(connection)` reflects portal tables `sites_siteurlscanconfiguration` (→ `sitelens_configured_scans_by_site`) and `sites_lighthousescanresult`, running a latest-timestamp subquery to load `accessibility_score/performance_score/best_practices_score/seo_score` into `sitelens_scores` keyed by `configuration_id`.
- `check_sitelens_urls(site_context)`: looks up the site in `sc.config['UMich']['portal']['sites']`; if fewer than 4 configured paths, calls `sc.add_notice({type:'info', csv:..., short:'add paths to SiteLens', message: &lt;a href=admin.webservices.umich.edu/sites/{id}/scan-configurations/&gt;}, site_context)`.
- `check_sitelens_scores(site_context)`: averages scores across scans, picks color by thresholds (`GOOD_SCORE_MIN=90`, `OK_SCORE_MIN=50`; colors `#00CC66`/`#FFAA33`/`#FF3333`), calls `create_gauge_image(value,color,title)` (matplotlib pie-chart gauge, 128×128 PNG to a `BytesIO` buffer). Each gauge is attached as an **inline image** with a `make_msgid(domain='webservices.umich.edu')` CID:
  ```python
  site_context['attachments'].append({'data': image,'maintype':'image','subtype':'png',
      'filename': f'pantheon_{site_name}_{key}_{sitelens_date}.png','cid': image_cid,'disposition':'inline'})
  ```
  and adds a **report section** `site_context['sections'].append({'heading':'SiteLens','content': &lt;table of &lt;img src="cid:..."&gt;&gt;, 'text': ...})`. Constants: `GAUGE_PIXELS_WIDTH/HEIGHT=128`, `score_ordering` iterates Accessibility/Performance/Best Practices/SEO. Test candidates: gauge color-threshold logic (pure), section/attachment assembly (integration with a fake `site_context` + mocked DB), render tier for the CID `&lt;img&gt;` HTML.

## 4. `docs/` directory

Two end-user docs (`/workspace/docs/`):
- `/workspace/docs/aws-credentials.md` — how to set up AWS credentials: shell vars, create an IAM policy, add a new IAM user + access key, store creds in 1Password (Vault "Pantheon Sitehealth Emails"), add user to group. This is the current per-person, least-privilege method.
- `/workspace/docs/awscli-login.md` — the **older** method using `awscli-login` (SAML/ECP against `weblogin.umich.edu`, Duo push, `aws login`). Explicitly marked as the legacy approach ("We used to run … Now, we are using per-person credentials").

No test-specific docs exist in `docs/` today.

## 5. `/workspace/README.md`

### Testing section (`## Testing`)
- pytest harness under `tests/`; full layout in `tests/README.md`.
- Install: `uv pip install .[test]` and `python -m playwright install --with-deps chromium` (headless Chromium for the render tier; "needs sudo for the system libraries").
- `./run-tests` wrapper flags: bare (everything incl. `live`, needs Terminus auth + network), `--fast` (offline: unit + integration + shim e2e + golden + render), `--llm` (terse machine-parseable summary), `--coverage` (no gate, in-process tiers only), `--update-goldens`, `--record` (re-record Terminus fixtures from live test site, read-only). Extra args pass through to pytest (`-k`, `-m`, paths).
- Marks/tiers: `unit`, `integration`, `e2e`, `live`, `render`, `email`, `slow`. `--fast` excludes `live` and `slow`. The `email` tier is a **deferred, skipped scaffold** (activates when email sending is re-enabled).
- **Two hard rules the harness enforces**: tests never run the program with `--all` or `--for-real` (a `run_program()` interlock refuses them); tests use only `its-wws-test1` / `its-wws-test2` test sites, read-only.

### First-time setup / PHP / credentials (`## Installation`)
- Python **3.13 and 3.12** supported; 3.11 untested-but-likely; **3.10 or earlier will not work**.
- **PHP + Composer** required for the **Emogrifier CSS processor** (`pelago/emogrifier`): `brew install php@8.4`; `composer install` pulls `vendor/`.
- **MySQL client** only if using MySQL instead of default SQLite3 (`pkgconf`, `mysql-client`; **U-M portal DB requires MySQL 8** — 5.x/9.x won't work → `mysql-client@8.4`).
- **AWS CLI** if using AWS (`aws configure --profile webhosting` or `AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID`/`AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY`).
- `uv`-managed Python 3.13 venv; `uv pip install .[mysql,aws,cloudflare]`; `python -m playwright install --with-deps chromium`; `composer install`.
- Usage section notes weekly `--update --all` (visitor counts) and monthly send flow with **Terminus machine token via ssh-add** (`ssh-add ~/.ssh/keys/pantheon-ecdsa256`) and the safety pattern: run one site, then `--all` (dry), then `--all --for-real`.

### TODO list (`## TO DO`) — items relevant to tests:
- "add SendGrid support as an additional option to SMTP → **Implement SMTP testing, GMail testing (see test harness prompt for requirements)**".
- `fqdns.json` get direct from Cloudflare; add `cf-cache-status`/`cache-control` checks; finish better secrets handling (Terminus machine token, SSH key, UMich Kerberos → SendGrid API key in AWS Secrets Manager, Cloudflare read-only token).
- "rework everything from ~3,700 line script into plugins and other Python packages"; refactor to fully use the plugin/config framework; switch to Pantheon API; `terminus()` → return tuple `(output, errors, fatal)`; check Live (not Dev) env for versions; env-lock report section; daily traffic alerts; move nightly traffic capture into portal app; accessibility-score notices; PHP memory in plan recs; % traffic cached by Cloudflare; security score in SiteLens.

## 6. Config templates

`/workspace/sample-pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml` (documented template). **Symlinks confirmed**:
```
local.toml -&gt; sample-pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml
pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml -&gt; pantheon-sitehealth-emails-config/pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml   # private repo
```
So the *active* config is a symlink into the private repo `its-webhosting/pantheon-sitehealth-emails-config`; the sample is the reusable template.

Sections relevant to tests:
- `[Pantheon]`: `org_id`, `overage_block_size = 10000`, `overage_block_cost = 40.00`.
- `[Pantheon.plan_info."&lt;Plan&gt;"]`: eight plans (Basic, Performance Small/Medium/Large/Extra Large/2X Large, Elite 1M, Elite 2M), each with `upgrade_at`, `upgrade_to`, `downgrade_to`, `traffic_limit`, `cost`. **These drive the report's plan recommendation logic** (prime target for unit/property tests on threshold boundaries).
- `[Pantheon.plan_sku_to_name]`: maps Pantheon SKUs (e.g. `plan-elite_1m-contract-annual-1`) → display names. Note the UMich portal plugin overwrites this at runtime.
- `[Database]`: `type` in {sqlite, mysql}; default `type="sqlite"`, `name="database.db"`; MySQL block (host/port/user/password/name) commented out. The `temp_db` fixture presumably exercises the SQLite path.
- `[Cloudflare]`: `enabled = false`; `member_email`/`member_api_key` fallbacks (overridden by env).
- `[AWS]`: `enabled = false`; `profile = "webhosting"`, `default_region = "us-east-1"` fallbacks.
- `[News]`: `folder = "./news"`; inline news items commented out (`order`, `icon`, `message`); items also loaded from `*.toml` in the folder.
- **No `[UMich]` section in the sample** — U-M-specific config (portal DB creds, `enabled=true`) lives only in the private config repo. Tests that exercise the umich plugin/check must supply their own `[UMich]` config (this is why the `minimal_config` fixture matters).

## 7. Jinja templates

`/workspace/email_template.html` (18,791 bytes, 457 lines) and `/workspace/email_template.txt` (5,825 bytes). Both rendered via `jinja2.Template(...).render(**template_dict)` (see main script lines ~3541/3550) into `build/&lt;site&gt;.{html,txt}`.

### `email_template.html` — headless-render-relevant facts
- **No JavaScript**: no `&lt;script&gt;` tags, no `on*` inline event handlers. So a headless render check should assert on layout/console-CSS, not JS behavior — but any console error would be CSS/resource-loading only.
- **Exactly one `&lt;style&gt;` block** (no external `&lt;link rel="stylesheet"&gt;`), `&lt;!DOCTYPE html&gt;`. The `&lt;style&gt;` is what **Emogrifier inlines**: pipeline is render → `build/&lt;site&gt;.html` → `inline-styles.php` (PHP Emogrifier from `vendor/`) → `build/&lt;site&gt;-inline.html` → `-inline2.html`. Render-tier tests should account for both the pre-inline (`&lt;style&gt;` present) and post-Emogrifier (styles inlined onto elements) forms.
- **Inline images via CID only** — two `&lt;img&gt;` with `src="cid:{{banner_cid}}"` (class `banner_image`) and `src="cid:{{chart_cid}}"` (class `chart_image`); SiteLens gauges add more CID images at runtime from `check/umich/sitelens.py`. A headless browser won't resolve `cid:` URIs, so broken-image warnings are expected unless CIDs are rewritten to data URIs/files for the render test.
- **Jinja control flow**: `{% if %}`×15 / `{% endif %}`×15, `{% for %}`×9 / `{% endfor %}`×9, `{% elif %}`×2, `{% else %}`×7 — meaning many conditional branches (notices, news items, plan recommendation, traffic table, cost table) that golden/render tests should cover across empty-and-populated states.
- **27 unique `{{ vars }}`**: `subject, banner_cid, dry_run_recipient, site_name, site_url, portal_site_id, notice.type, notice.icon, notice.message, item.message, section.heading, section.content, current_plan, recommended_plan, median_monthly_visitors, months_until_recommendations, chart_cid, column['name'], column['label'], current_month_estimate, traffic_date, traffic_table_rows[row]['month'], traffic_table_rows[row][column['name']], estimate_start_date, estimate_end_date, cost_table_rows[row]['plan'], cost_table_rows[row][column['name']]`.
- **Email-client CSS caveats baked into comments** (matter for render/CSS tests): a workaround for clients without `nth-of-type` ("particularly GMail and Outlook"); a note that "Thunderbird strips out media queries starting in Thunderbird 78 … As of Thunderbird 115 (June 2024)"; `.responsive-table` uses `!important` overrides and `display: block` breakpoints. The responsive table adapts via media queries — a render test at different viewport widths would exercise these.

### `email_template.txt`
Plaintext counterpart (~5.8 KB) rendered from the same `template_dict` (main script line ~3550). Mirrors sections/notices/traffic/cost tables in plain text; `section.text` (auto-generated via `html2text` when absent) feeds it. Golden tests should snapshot both `.html` (and its inlined form) and `.txt`.

---

# `pantheon-sitehealth-emails` — Functional Map for Test Planning

Two source files: `/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails` (3702 lines, extension-less, imported/run as the main module) and `/workspace/script_context.py` (92 lines, imported as `sc`). Note: `main()` is a single monolithic function spanning **lines 776–3697** with **no nested `def`s** — the entire per-site pipeline is inline, which is the dominant testability obstacle.

Existing test scaffolding already present: `/workspace/tests/` with tiers unit/integration/e2e/render/live/email, `conftest.py`, terminus fixtures, syrupy goldens, a `terminus` shim, and `/workspace/run-tests` (pytest wrapper). Markers/tiers defined in `/workspace/pyproject.toml` lines 41–52.

---

## 1. `script_context.py` — the `sc` shared-state module

Module-level mutable state (all reassigned at runtime by `main()`):
- `options = {}` (L9) — parsed CLI namespace; set from `__main__` via `sc.options = parse_args()`.
- `config = {}` (L10) — parsed TOML, reassigned repeatedly by `process_config`.
- `plugin = {}` (L11) — imported plugin modules keyed by dotted name (e.g. `"plugin.cloudflare"`).
- `check = {}` (L12) — imported check modules.
- `news = []` (L13) — global list of news-item dicts (shared across all sites; never reset per-site).
- `console = Console()` (L16) — Rich console.
- `substitutions = []` (L18) — list of `{"args": [...], "func_args": [...], "func": callable}` registered by plugins; consumed by `config_substitution`.
- `hooks = {'setup': [], 'check': []}` (L20–23) — hook registry.
- `plugin_context = {}` (L25).
- `icon = {'info','warning','alert'}` (L27–31) — HTML entity strings.
- `text_maker` (L54–63) — configured `html2text.HTML2Text()` instance used to auto-derive plaintext from HTML.

Helpers (verbatim signatures + behavior):
- `def debug(*args, level: int = 1) -&gt; None` (L34) — logs via `console.log` only if `options.verbose &gt;= level`. Note it reads `options.verbose` as an **attribute**, so `options` must be a Namespace, not the `{}` default.
- `def add_hook(hook_name: str, target: dict) -&gt; None` (L39) — appends `target` to `hooks[hook_name]`, creating the key if absent.
- `def invoke_hooks(hook_name: str, *args, **kwargs) -&gt; None` (L46) — iterates `hooks[hook_name]`, calling each `hook['func'](*args, **kwargs)`; reads `hook['name']` for debug. No return, no error handling.
- `def add_notice(notice: dict, site_context: dict) -&gt; None` (L65) — requires `'message'` key (else `console.print` + `sys.exit(1)`); defaults `icon` from `icon[notice['type']]`, `text` from `text_maker.handle(message)`; inserts at front if `order` in `('prepend','first')` else appends to `site_context['notices']`.
- `def add_news_item(news_item: dict, from_where: str = 'check') -&gt; None` (L80) — same shape as `add_notice` but appends/prepends to the **global** `news` list; `sys.exit(1)` if `'message'` missing.

Good unit targets here: `add_hook`, `invoke_hooks`, `add_notice`, `add_news_item` (icon/text defaulting, order semantics, missing-message exit).

---

## 2. Main script `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`

### 2a. Entry / arg parsing
- `def build_arg_parser() -&gt; argparse.ArgumentParser` (L145) — `allow_abbrev=False`. Args: positional `sites` (nargs `*`); `--all/-a`; `--date/-d` (type `datetime.date.fromisoformat`, default today); `--update`; `--for-real`; `--config/-c` (default `pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml`); `--only-warn`; `--smtp-username/-u` (default `os.environ.get("USER","")`); `--create-tables`; `--import-older-metrics`; `--verbose/-v` (count). **Side-effect-free.**
- `def parse_args(argv=None)` (L229) — `return build_arg_parser().parse_args(argv)`. Clean unit seam.
- `if __name__ == "__main__":` (L3700) — sets `sc.options = parse_args()` then `main()`. Module is import-safe (no argv side effects at import).
- `def main() -&gt; None` (L776).

### 2b. `main()` pipeline (top → bottom)
1. Load TOML → `sc.config` (L778–780).
2. Import plugins via `find_modules("plugin")` (L782–786).
3. **First** `process_config` pass — "pre-setup" (L788–789).
4. Import checks via `find_modules("check")` (L791–795).
5. Arg validation (L797–807): `--create-tables` forces `verbose=3` and is mutually exclusive with `--import-older-metrics`; must supply either sites or `--all`.
6. Create `build/` dir (L813–815).
7. `sc.invoke_hooks("setup")` (L817) — plugins register substitutions/hooks here.
8. **Second** `process_config` pass — "post-setup" (L819–820). Runs twice so that plugin-registered substitutions (added during the setup hook) resolve on the second pass.
9. Read `overage_block_size`/`overage_block_cost` (L825–826).
10. DB selection (L832–842): `sqlite` → `sqlite:///{name}`; `mysql` → `mysql+mysqldb://…` with `pool_size=10, max_overflow=20`; else `sys.exit`. `create_engine` (L844, `echo` when verbose≥2), `sessionmaker`, `db_session` (L849–850).
11. `--create-tables`: `Base.metadata.create_all(db_engine)` then `sys.exit("Tables created.")` (L852–854).
12. Read `header-image.png` → `wordmark_image` (L856–857).
13. News loading (L863–882) — see 2f.
14. Plan_info normalization + alias (L884–896) — see 2e.
15. Date math (L898–906): `end_date = options.date`; `start_date` = first of same month one year prior; `end_of_contract_year` True if June 16–29.
16. Cap-shape geometry for surge bars (L908–916, numpy).
17. `sites = terminus("org:site:list", org_id)` (L918); build `site_name_to_id` (L930).
18. **Per-site loop** `for site_name in sorted(site_name_to_id.keys())` (L933) → ends L3666; `db_session.close()` L3671.
    - UMich portal gate (L941–951, guarded).
    - Skip non-selected sites (L953–958); Elite SKU resolution (L970–984); skip Sandbox (L990–992).
    - Metrics fetch + DB upsert (L1080–1155) — see 2g.
    - Domain/DNS/Cloudflare checks (L1201–1418, `fqdn_re`, `dns.resolver`, `ipaddress`).
    - WP/Drupal plugin/module checks incl. U-M-specific ones (L1553–1650, 2093–2150).
    - `sc.invoke_hooks("check", site_context)` (L1181) — where check modules (incl. SiteLens gauges) inject sections/attachments.
    - Traffic aggregation, plan-over-time, estimate (L2543–2637).
    - Surge chart (L2640–2965) — see 2h.
    - Overage-protection table build + upsert (L2985–3091) — see 2g.
    - Plan recommendation (L3105–3295) — see 2e.
    - UMich billing notices (L3382–3531, guarded), rendering + MIME (L3533–3653) — see 2h.
19. Post-loop CSV/JSON output when `--all` (L3674–3695); savings summary.

### 2c. Terminus / WP / Drush wrappers
- `def run_terminus(command: list, input_data=None) -&gt; (str, str, bool)` (L237) — prepends `["terminus","--no-ansi","--no-interaction", …]`; `subprocess.Popen` with **300 s timeout** (L259); on `TimeoutExpired` kills and returns `(output, errors, True)` (L260–269). Heavy output/error filtering for `wp`/`composer` (L274–313). Returns `(output, errors, fatal)`; `fatal=True` on nonzero return (L318–322).
- `def terminus(*args) -&gt; Any` (L327) — appends `--format=json`; **retry logic**: sentinel `"pshe-no-retry"` (L335); on `"Invalid or expired session header"` sleeps 5 s and retries once (L347–351). **Returns only `result`** — drops `errors`/`fatal` (TODO at L352). On JSON decode error sets `result = ""` (L343, TODO None). Callers index into the result directly.
- `def wp(siteenv, *args) -&gt; (Any, str)` (L356) — `wp … --format=json`; returns `(result, errors, fatal)` (docstring signature `(Any,str)` is stale — actually 3-tuple).
- `def wp_eval(siteenv, *args) -&gt; (str, str)` (L370) — `wp … eval …`; returns `(output.strip(), errors.strip(), fatal)` (also actually a 3-tuple).
- `def wp_error(site, code, message, errors) -&gt; list[dict]` (L379) — builds an alert notice dict list (html + text + csv).
- `def fix_drush_output(output, errors) -&gt; (str, str)` (L405) — moves leading non-JSON lines from output into errors. Pure-ish, good unit target.
- `def drush(siteenv, *args) -&gt; (Any, str)` (L427) — `drush … --format=json`; runs `fix_drush_output`; returns `(result, errors, fatal)`.
- `def drush_php_script(siteenv, script) -&gt; (Any, str)` (L442) — `drush … php:script --format=json -` with `input_data=script`.
- `def drush_error(site, code, message, errors) -&gt; list[dict]` (L457) — Drush analogue of `wp_error`.
- `def escape_url(url)` (L233) — `urllib.parse.quote(url, safe=":/?#&amp;=", …)`. Pure, unit target.

### 2d. Plugin/check discovery
- `def find_modules(module_type: str) -&gt; list[str]` (L753) — `os.walk(module_type, followlinks=True)`; collects dirs containing a non-empty regular `__init__.py`; converts path to dotted module name via `"/".join`→`".".join`; sorted. Depends on CWD and `sys.path`. Discovers `/workspace/plugin/{cloudflare,aws,umich}` and `/workspace/check/umich` (which contains `sitelens.py`).

### 2e. Config substitution + plan recommendation
- `def config_substitution(expr: str, path) -&gt; str` (L667) — tokenizes with `shlex`; scores each `sc.substitutions` entry by prefix match with `$`-wildcards; calls the best match's `func` with mapped args; `sys.exit(1)` on unknown/no-match/None-result. Complex scoring — strong unit target (feed synthetic `sc.substitutions`).
- `config_substitution_re = re.compile(r"&lt;\{(.*?)(?&lt;!\\)}")` (L732) — the `&lt;{ … }&gt;` mechanism (matches `&lt;{ expr }` with non-escaped closing brace).
- `def process_config(data, path="") -&gt; Any` (L735) — recursively walks dict/list/str; `re.sub` replaces each `&lt;{…}&gt;` via `config_substitution`. Runs twice (L789, L820) around the setup hook. Recursive, mutating.
- **Plan recommendation** — spread across `main()`, not a function:
  - Normalization (L884–892): `"-"` sentinels in `upgrade_to`/`downgrade_to` → `None`.
  - Cost model (L3113–3169): for each plan, `cost_same` = annual cost + summed monthly overage (overage blocks = `round((overage + block_size/2)/block_size)`), factoring PantheonOverageProtection waivers (L3127–3143); short histories extrapolated with median (L3148–3149). `costs_median` (L3158–3168) = base cost + median-traffic overage × `months_without_op` (12 for Basic, else 8).
  - Selection (L3171–3175): `costs_best[p] = max(cost_same[p], costs_median[p])` (conservative); `site_recommended_plan = min(costs_best, key=costs_best.get)`.
  - Downgrade guardrails (L3185–3235): Basic special-casing, "Performance Small" floor, intermediate-plan search excluding Basic.
  - Only computed when `len(v) &gt; 4` (&gt;4 months of data); `months_until_recommendations = 0 if len(v)&gt;4 else 5-len(v)` (L3109).

### 2f. Notices / news loading
- Config-based news (L863–870): iterates `sc.config["News"].keys()`, calls `sc.add_news_item`. **BUG (see §5): the `if not isinstance(news_item_name, dict): continue` guard is always true**, so this loop never adds anything.
- File-based news (L871–879): globs `f"{sc.config['News']['folder']}/*.toml"` (from `[News].folder`, sample `./news`), requires top-level `[News]` table, calls `add_news_item(..., f"{name} in file {filename}")`.
- Site notices: `check_wordpress_plugin` (L547), `check_drupal_module` (L615), `wp_error`/`drush_error`, and inline appends into `site_notices`; later sorted alert→warning→info (L3402–3406).

### 2g. Database — models + upsert
- `class PantheonTraffic(Base)` (L97) — table `pantheon_traffic`; cols `site_id CHAR(36)`, `traffic_date Date`, `site_plan String(64)`, `visits`, `pages_served`, `cache_hits` Integer; composite PK + unique on `(site_id, traffic_date)`.
- `class PantheonOverageProtection(Base)` (L120) — table `pantheon_overage_protection`; cols `site_id CHAR(36)`, `month Date`, `months_remaining Integer`, `used_this_month Boolean`; composite PK/unique on `(site_id, month)`.
- Daily upsert (L1095–1112): `db_session.merge(PantheonTraffic(...))` per timeseries entry (skips `traffic_date == end_date`, today's partial). 
- Bulk import (`--import-older-metrics`, L1114–1151): sqlite → `sqlite_insert(...).on_conflict_do_nothing(index_elements=["site_id","traffic_date"])`; mysql → `insert(...).prefix_with("IGNORE")`; rows from `get_old_metrics` (L483, distributes weekly/monthly totals to days). Then `continue`.
- Overage-protection upsert (L2989–3091): `db_session.get(...)` then `add`/update `months_remaining`/`used_this_month`; retroactive start `month &gt;= "2024-01"`, 4-month January reset, Basic excluded; commit at L3091.
- `--create-tables` at L852.

### 2h. Rendering / charts / MIME / SMTP
- **Jinja2** (L3536–3578): `template_dict` assembled (L3536–3565), `email_template.html` and `email_template.txt` read and rendered with `jinja2.Template`; written to `build/{site}.html` and `.txt`.
- **inline-styles.php** (L3582–3592): `subprocess.run(["php","inline-styles.php", in, out], check=True)`; then output re-read (L3593) and every CSS `;` gets ` !important;` appended via regex (L3596–3602).
- **matplotlib** (core = **traffic surge bar chart only**, L2640–2965): GridSpec 2-panel "broken axis" when `surge` (visits_max &gt; `upgrade_at_max*1.5`); bars, cap-shape `Polygon`s (L2780–2803), estimate label, `fig.savefig(buf, format="png")` → `chart_image = buf.read()` (L2960–2963); `plt.close(fig)`. **There are NO SiteLens gauges in the core script** — SiteLens gauge charts live in the check module `/workspace/check/umich/sitelens.py`, injected as `site_context["sections"]`/`attachments` via the `"check"` hook (L1181). Worth confirming when planning chart tests.
- **CIDs**: `banner_cid`/`chart_cid = make_msgid(domain="webservices.umich.edu")` (L3533–3534); passed to template stripped of `&lt;&gt;` (`[1:-1]`, L3563–3564).
- **MIME assembly** (L3607–3653): `EmailMessage`; `set_content(text_body)` + `add_alternative(html_body, subtype="html")`; `add_related` for wordmark (banner_cid), chart (chart_cid), and each `site_context["attachments"]`; written to `build/{site}.eml` via `msg.as_bytes(policy=SMTP)`. 
- **SMTP send is DISABLED/commented out — CONFIRMED**: `def smtp_login()` (L769) exists but the only calls are commented (L3656–3659 and L860–861); `emails_sent` is never incremented (the `emails_sent += 1` at L3658 is commented), so the L3676 "Email sent for N sites" always reports 0.

---

## 3. Pure / near-pure helper functions (best unit-test candidates)

| Function | Line | Nature |
|---|---|---|
| `escape_url(url)` | 233 | pure URL quoting |
| `fix_drush_output(output, errors)` | 405 | pure string reshaping (JSON-boundary detection) |
| `wp_error(site, code, message, errors)` | 379 | pure dict-list builder |
| `drush_error(site, code, message, errors)` | 457 | pure dict-list builder |
| `check_wordpress_plugin(...)` | 547 | near-pure (only side effect = `console.print`); returns notice list |
| `check_drupal_module(...)` | 615 | near-pure, same shape |
| `config_substitution(expr, path)` | 667 | pure given injected `sc.substitutions` (calls `sys.exit` on failure) |
| `process_config(data)` | 735 | pure recursion over data + regex |
| `build_arg_parser()` / `parse_args()` | 145 / 229 | side-effect-free parser construction |
| `get_old_metrics(...)` | 483 | pure given a metrics dict (date/visit distribution math) — **but** calls `terminus()` internally at L487, so needs that seam stubbed |
| `find_modules(module_type)` | 753 | filesystem-pure (walk) |
| `sc.add_notice` / `sc.add_news_item` / `sc.add_hook` / `sc.invoke_hooks` | script_context 39–92 | small, pure-ish |
| `PantheonTraffic.__repr__` / `PantheonOverageProtection.__repr__` | 113 / 133 | trivial |

Pure **math/formatting logic worth extracting-and-testing** (currently inline in `main()`, not callable): date math (L898–905, `end_of_contract_year`), overage-block rounding (L3036–3039, `round((overage+block/2)/block)`), estimate extrapolation (L2617–2637), plan cost/selection (L3113–3175), surge threshold (`upgrade_at_max*1.5`, L2646), byte/number formatting is all `f"{x:,.0f}"` / `f"${x:,.2f}"` (no dedicated formatter helper). `fqdn_re` (L90) domain validation is testable as a regex.

---

## 4. Institution-specific (U-M) code NOT behind `[UMich].enabled`

Only **four** blocks are properly guarded by the `"UMich" in sc.config and …["enabled"]` idiom: **L941–951, L3382–3392, L3412–3486, L3498–3531**. Everything below is U-M-hardcoded in the CORE script and runs regardless of any `[UMich].enabled` flag — latent bugs for any non-U-M deployment:

- **L771** `smtp_login()` — hardcoded `SMTP_SSL("smtp.mail.umich.edu", port=465)` and `os.environ["SMTP_PASSWORD"]`.
- **L1569–1577** `umich-cloudflare` plugin check ("University of Michigan: Cloudflare Cache", `documentation.its.umich.edu/node/5114`) — gated only by `len(fqdns_behind_cloudflare) &gt; 0`, not by UMich.enabled.
- **L1595–1650** `umich-oidc-login` reinstall special-case check (semver compare, GitHub release URLs, U-M shortcode text) — inside the generic plugins loop, unguarded.
- **L2093 / L2137–2150** Drupal user-agent check pointing at `documentation.its.umich.edu/node/4242` (uses `ifconfig.me/ua`) — unguarded U-M content.
- **L1014, L1024** notice HTML/text with `its.umich.edu/computing/web-mobile/pantheon/support` — baked into a general notice string.
- **L1429–1471** Cloudflare "at U-M" documentation URLs inside Cloudflare-domain notices.
- **L3533–3534** `make_msgid(domain="webservices.umich.edu")` — unconditional, every site.
- **L3607–3617 MIME headers (all unconditional):** `From: University of Michigan Webmaster Team &lt;webmaster@umich.edu&gt;` (L3608); dry-run `To: januside@go.mail.umich.edu, {smtp_username}@umich.edu` (L3611–3614); `Bcc: januside@…, its-webmaster@…` (L3611); `Reply-to: webmaster@umich.edu` (L3617).
- (Guarded, but note the hardcoded site names) **L3390–3392** special-cases `"lsa-disko-project"`, `"umma-inside-wp"` — inside the UMich guard, but still string-literal site names.

The two comments at L3410–3411 and L3494–3497 document that previous `if True:` blocks here crashed non-U-M runs with `KeyError('UMich')` and were retrofitted with the guard — evidence the guarding effort is incomplete and the pattern is bug-prone.

---

## 5. Code smells / bugs / fragile spots (with file:line)

**Likely real bugs**
- **Dead config-news loop** — `pantheon-sitehealth-emails:865`: `for news_item_name in sc.config["News"].keys(): if not isinstance(news_item_name, dict): continue`. Keys are strings, so the `continue` always fires → the config-defined News items (L867–870) are never added. Only file-based news (L871) works.
- **Possible `NameError: median_visitors`** — `:3555` uses `median_monthly_visitors=f"{median_visitors:,.0f}"` unconditionally, but `median_visitors` is only assigned at `:3155` inside `if len(v) &gt; 4:`. Sites with ≤4 months of data reach rendering without it defined (unless an earlier iteration leaked the name — fragile cross-iteration reliance).
- **`emails_sent` always 0** — increment at `:3658` is commented out, but `:3676` prints "Email sent for {emails_sent} of {site_count} sites." Misleading output while SMTP is disabled.
- **Stale/incorrect option name in comment/logic** — `:3666` `plt.close(fig) # … when sc.options.all_sites is True`; the option is `all`, not `all_sites`.

**Silent failure / error-swallowing**
- **`terminus()` drops errors and fatal flag** — `:352–353` returns only `result`; TODOs at L343 (`result = ""` instead of `None`) and L352. Callers index directly (e.g. `terminus("plan:info", …)["sku"]` at L972–978; `["timeseries"]` at L490/L1081/L1095) → on decode failure `result=""` yields `""["sku"]` = `TypeError`, or empty-dict iteration silently produces no rows.
- **DNS exceptions swallowed** — `:1252–1258` and `:1282–1288` catch `NoAnswer/NXDOMAIN/NoNameservers/Timeout` and (per surrounding code) largely `continue`/pass, so DNS failures silently skip domain checks.
- **`wp`/`wp_eval`/`drush` docstrings' return signatures are wrong** — declared `-&gt; (Any, str)` / `-&gt; (str, str)` at L356/370/427 but they actually return 3-tuples `(result, errors, fatal)`; callers must unpack 3 (see L1685 `ocp_config, errors, fatal = wp_eval(...)`).

**Fragile / smell**
- **Popen attribute mutation** — `:292` `p.returncode = 0` overwrites a live `Popen` attribute to force success for composer.
- **Backslash inside f-string expressions** — `:385` and `:463` `json.dumps(errors).replace(',', '\\,')` require Python ≥3.12 f-string semantics; brittle on older interpreters (project requires ≥3.11 per pyproject L4).
- **`echo=True` on the DB engine when verbose≥2** — `:846` will dump all SQL, including the mysql password present in the conn string `:837`.
- **CWD-dependent behavior** — `find_modules` (L756), `build/` creation (L814), template opens (`email_template.html/.txt`), `header-image.png` (L856), `inline-styles.php` (L3585) all assume the process runs from the repo root.
- **Unbounded `terminus` retry recursion is bounded only by the `pshe-no-retry` sentinel** (L335, L350) — fine, but the recursion + list-mutation pattern (fixed per the L331–333 comment) is subtle.
- **Broad `terminus` output filtering by string matching** (L283–313) — brittle heuristics on human-readable Terminus warnings.
- **Global mutable `sc.news`** accumulates across the whole run (not per-site) — correct by design, but any per-site test must account for cross-test leakage of `sc.news`, `sc.config`, `sc.substitutions`, `sc.plugin`, `sc.check`.

**Testability note for planning:** the wrappers `run_terminus` (subprocess), `terminus` (the single network seam most tests mock — see `tests/integration/test_terminus_seam.py` and `tests/fixtures/terminus/*.json`), the two Jinja templates + `inline-styles.php` (real PHP dependency in e2e), and the SQLAlchemy models are your four integration seams. The pure helpers in §3 are the cleanest unit targets; the plan-recommendation and overage-protection math (currently inline in `main()`) are the highest-value logic but require either refactoring into functions or exercising through the e2e/golden path.</result>

</task-notification>

## Assistant

Verified the load-bearing facts:

- **`median_visitors` bug is real and blocking.** It's assigned only inside `if len(v) > 4:` (L3155) but consumed unconditionally when building `template_dict` (L3555) — as are `site_current_plan_index`/`site_recommended_plan_index` (assigned even deeper, inside `if site["plan_name"] != site_recommended_plan:`). Any site with ≤4 months of traffic (i.e. a new site) `NameError`s during rendering. The current golden passes only because its-wws-test1's recorded metrics supply >4 months. Testing the new-site path requires fixing this first — matches your "fix blocking bugs now" call.
- **Dead config-news loop confirmed** (L864–866: iterates string keys, `if not isinstance(..., dict): continue` always fires).
- **`--create-tables`/`--import-older-metrics` DB risk confirmed** (L852–854 runs `create_all` against whatever `[Database]` points at — production MySQL if the real config is loaded). Your constraint is well-founded; I'll enforce it in the interlock.

```json
{
  "file_path": "/home/node/.claude/plans/development-2026-07-04-test-suite-promp-twinkling-brook.md",
  "content": "# Plan: Test-suite specification for `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`\n\n## Context\n\nA pytest harness was just built (`development/2026-07-04-test-harness/SPEC.md`) with basic\nsmoke tests proving the harness works. This task is the **design/specification** step for the\nreal test suite that will cover the program's existing functionality — so that the upcoming\nwork (re-enabling SMTP + adding SendGrid, new features, de-monolithing `main()`, moving logic\ninto the plugin/config frameworks) has a safety net that catches regressions early.\n\nPer the driving prompt (`development/2026-07-04-test-suite/PROMPT.md`), **this session produces\nthe design artifacts only — it does not implement the tests.** The deliverables of executing\nthis plan are:\n\n1. `development/2026-07-04-test-suite/SPEC.md` — the complete, implementation-ready test spec\n   (the permanent in-repo design record; the user may hand-edit it before implementation).\n2. `development/2026-07-04-test-suite/PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md` — program bugs found during\n   design, logged for a later fix session (not fixed now, except the one blocking bug below).\n3. An adversarial spec-review pass (independent reviewer subagent, ≤3 iterations) with results\n   reported back.\n\nTests, the refactor, and the bug fix described below are **implemented in a later session** from\nthe approved SPEC.md — not in this one.\n\nThe suite must **extend the existing harness and honor its hard safety constraints** — no\nparallel testing approach.\n\n## Non-negotiable safety constraints (design-time and every run, now and future)\n\n- **NEVER** `--all` / `-a` (up-to-6-hour full run) and **NEVER** `--for-real` (sends real\n  customer email). Already enforced by `run_program()`'s `ForbiddenFlagError` interlock\n  (`tests/conftest.py`).\n- **NEVER run `--create-tables` or `--import-older-metrics` \"live\"** (against the real config /\n  production MySQL). Only ever against a throwaway temp SQLite DB in offline mode. *New this\n  plan* — see Part C.\n- Tests use only `its-wws-test1` (WordPress) and `its-wws-test2` (Drupal), read-only.\n- No SMTP re-enable, no SMTP tests, no GMail/SendGrid tests — all deferred to a future session.\n  The `email` tier stays a skipped scaffold.\n\n## Decisions locked with the user (interview)\n\n| Decision | Choice |\n|---|---|\n| Refactor for testability | **Extract key pure helpers** from `main()` (behavior-preserving, golden-pinned) |\n| Discovered bugs | **Fix only truly-blocking bugs now**, log the rest to PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md |\n| Drupal coverage | **Yes** — record `its-wws-test2` fixtures + a second Drupal golden |\n| Render tier depth | **Functional + console-error + axe-core a11y smoke** (no pixel screenshots) |\n| Plugin tests | **All three**: AWS `get_secret`, Cloudflare `ips`, UMich portal + SiteLens (mock-based) |\n| Lower-effort extras | **All four**: MIME/.eml structural, config-substitution engine, argparse contract, Hypothesis property on extracted helpers |\n| CI | **No** — local `./run-tests` only |\n| Mutation testing | **No** |\n\n## Explicitly NOT in scope (record so it's not silently dropped)\n\n- The `--all` aggregation/CSV/JSON post-loop path (L3674–3695) — unreachable without `--all`.\n- Any real SMTP/SendGrid send path; the commented-out `smtp_login()` send.\n- GMail rendering/deliverability tests (future session).\n- CI workflow, mutation testing, pixel/visual-regression screenshots.\n- Full de-monolithing of `main()` — only the four extractions below are pulled forward.\n- Live `--create-tables` / `--import-older-metrics`.\n\n---\n\n## Part A — Behavior-preserving extractions (prerequisite for unit/property tests)\n\nKeep the \"one big file\" convention: define these as **module-level functions in the main\n`pantheon-sitehealth-emails` script** (so tests import them as `psh.<fn>`), and call them from\n`main()`. Pin behavior with the existing golden e2e (must stay byte-identical after extraction,\nmodulo the intended bug fix in Part B).\n\n1. **`overage_blocks(overage, block_size) -> int`** — the `round((overage + block/2)/block)`\n   rounding used at L3123 and L3165. Pure. High-value boundary tests.\n2. **`contract_year_end(report_date) -> bool`** — the \"June 16–29\" end-of-contract-year check\n   (L900–906). Pure. (U-M-specific semantics but harmless/general as a date predicate.)\n3. **`estimate_month_visits(...) -> float`** — the current-month traffic extrapolation\n   (L2617–2637). Pure given its inputs.\n4. **`recommend_plan(...) -> dict`** — the cost model + selection + downgrade guardrails\n   (L3105–3295). **Decouple from the DB**: inject overage-protection data as a plain\n   `dict[str, OPRecord]` or a `Callable[[str_month], op|None]`, not a live `db_session`.\n   Returns a complete result dict: `recommended_plan`, `median_visitors`, `cost_same`,\n   `costs_median`, `costs_best`, `current_plan_index`, `recommended_plan_index`,\n   `months_until_recommendations`, `cost_table_rows`. **Always returns a complete dict, even\n   for ≤4-month sites** (this is where the Part B fix lives).\n\n`main()` changes to call these; the surrounding DB reads (`db_session.get(PantheonOverageProtection, …)`)\nare gathered into the injected op-lookup before the call.\n\n## Part B — The one blocking bug fix (folded into the `recommend_plan` extraction)\n\nFor sites with ≤4 months of traffic, `main()` builds `template_dict` (L3555, L3544–3545) using\n`median_visitors`, `site_current_plan_index`, `site_recommended_plan_index` — all assigned only\ninside `if len(v) > 4:` (and, for the indices, only inside the \"current != recommended\" branch).\nResult: `NameError` when rendering any new site. This blocks testing the (valid, common)\nnew-site path, so it is fixed now.\n\n**Fix:** `recommend_plan` returns sensible defaults for the ≤4-month case — `median_visitors = 0`\n(or the mean of available months), indices default to the current plan's index, empty\n`cost_table_rows`, `months_until_recommendations = 5 - len(v)`. `main()` reads these off the\nreturned dict, so the unconditional `template_dict` construction is always well-defined. A new\nregression test (`its-wws-test1` with ≤4 months seeded) asserts render succeeds and the template\nshows the \"not enough data yet\" state.\n\nAll **other** discovered bugs are logged to PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md and left in place; where a\npath is currently broken but not blocking, a **strict-xfail** test documents intended behavior\nand auto-alerts when the bug is later fixed.\n\n## Part C — Safety-interlock hardening (`tests/conftest.py`)\n\nExtend `_assert_flags_allowed` / `run_program` so `--create-tables` and `--import-older-metrics`\nare **refused whenever the run is not offline** — i.e. blocked in `mode=\"live\"` and blocked\nunless the effective `--config` is a test fixture config whose `[Database]` is a temp SQLite\npath. Fail-closed with a named exception (extend `ForbiddenFlagError` or add\n`ForbiddenLiveDataError`). Add unit tests mirroring `tests/unit/test_interlock.py`. This makes\nthe \"never touch production data\" rule structural, not a convention.\n\n---\n\n## Part D — Test inventory by tier\n\nAll tests reuse existing fixtures (`psh`, `reset_sc`, `temp_db`, `program_runner`/`run_program`,\n`rendered_report`, `normalize_html`, `forbidden_flag_error`) and import constants\n`from conftest import …`. New per-tier files below.\n\n### unit (`tests/unit/`, mark `unit`) — pure, in-process\n- **`test_plan_math.py`** — `overage_blocks` boundary tests (0, exactly one block, half-block\n  rounding up/down, huge overage); `contract_year_end` across the June 16–29 edges and\n  non-June dates; `estimate_month_visits` mid-month/edge inputs.\n- **`test_recommend_plan.py`** — parametrized example tests over crafted `plan_info` +\n  `visits_by_month`: below all limits → cheapest plan; sustained overage → upgrade; overage-\n  protection waiver zeroing cost; downgrade guardrails (Basic special-case, \"Performance Small\"\n  floor, intermediate search); the ≤4-month \"not enough data\" result shape (Part B).\n- **`test_config_substitution.py`** — `config_substitution` / `process_config`: `<{ … }>`\n  resolution, `shlex` tokenizing, `$`-wildcard scoring/best-match, twice-run pass semantics,\n  `sys.exit` on unknown/no-match/None result (assert via `pytest.raises(SystemExit)`).\n- **`test_argparse_contract.py`** — `build_arg_parser`: `--create-tables` vs\n  `--import-older-metrics` mutual exclusion; sites-or-`--all` requirement; `--date`\n  `fromisoformat` parse + failure; `allow_abbrev=False` rejects `--fo`/`--al`; defaults\n  (`--smtp-username` from `$USER`, `--config` default, `--verbose` count).\n- **`test_interlock.py`** (extend existing) — add `--create-tables`/`--import-older-metrics`\n  live-refusal cases (Part C).\n- **`test_pure_functions.py`** / **`test_property.py`** (extend existing) — keep `escape_url`,\n  `fix_drush_output`.\n\n### property (in `tests/unit/`, mark `unit`) — Hypothesis\n- **`test_property_plan.py`** — over `overage_blocks` (monotonic non-decreasing in overage,\n  non-negative, `overage=0 → 0`); `recommend_plan` invariants (returns a valid plan name;\n  `costs_best[p] == max(cost_same[p], costs_median[p])`; recommended plan has min `costs_best`;\n  never crashes on 0…N months incl. the ≤4 path).\n\n### integration (`tests/integration/`, mark `integration`) — monkeypatch `run_terminus`, `temp_db`\n- **`test_terminus_seam.py`** / **`test_regressions.py`** (existing) — keep.\n- **`test_wrappers.py`** — `terminus()` session-expiry retry (already regressed) + JSON-decode\n  path; `wp`/`wp_eval`/`drush`/`drush_php_script` return-tuple shapes `(result, errors, fatal)`;\n  `wp_error`/`drush_error` notice dict-list shape; `fix_drush_output` leading-noise handling.\n- **`test_db_roundtrip.py`** — `PantheonTraffic` and `PantheonOverageProtection` upsert/merge\n  semantics against `temp_db` (idempotent re-run, unique-constraint on `(site_id, date/month)`).\n- **`test_mime_structure.py`** — parse `rendered_report['eml']`: assert `multipart/alternative`\n  + `related` structure, a non-empty plaintext alternative, and **every `cid:` referenced in the\n  HTML has a matching related part and vice-versa** (CID integrity).\n\n### plugin tests (`tests/integration/`, mark `integration`) — all mock-based, no live calls\n- **`test_plugin_aws.py`** — mock boto3 (`botocore.Stubber`): Secrets Manager fetch, JSON\n  decode, base64 `SecretBinary`, module-level cache hit, `KeyError` on missing key.\n- **`test_plugin_cloudflare.py`** — mock the `Cloudflare` client: CIDR strings →\n  `ipaddress.ip_network` for v4/v6; `sys.exit` on client failure.\n- **`test_plugin_umich_portal.py`** — temp SQLite engine standing in for the portal DB: reflect\n  `sites_site`/`sites_pantheonplan`; assert `plan_sku_to_name` runtime override; setup-hook\n  ordering (`setup` → `setup.umich.portal` → `check`).\n- **`test_check_sitelens.py`** — gauge color-threshold logic (pure: GOOD≥90, OK≥50, else red);\n  section/attachment assembly against a synthetic `site_context` + mocked scores; assert an\n  inline PNG attachment with a `cid` and a \"SiteLens\" section are added.\n\n### e2e (`tests/e2e/`, mark `e2e`) — shim/replay, offline, temp SQLite\n- **`test_shim_e2e.py`** / **`test_golden.py`** (existing WordPress) — keep; add the **≤4-month\n  new-site** case asserting render succeeds and the \"not enough data yet\" template state.\n- **`test_golden_drupal.py`** + **`__snapshots__/test_golden_drupal.ambr`** — new **Drupal**\n  golden for `its-wws-test2` (drush path), HTML (CID-normalized) + `.txt`.\n\n### render (`tests/render/`, mark `render`) — Playwright, skips if Chromium unavailable\n- **`test_render.py`** (rework) — rewrite `cid:` images to `data:` URIs so images actually load;\n  assert **zero console errors**; assert key structural elements/layout present (title, banner\n  img `naturalWidth>0`, chart img, notices/news/traffic/cost sections across empty+populated);\n  run an **axe-core** accessibility smoke check (inject axe from a vendored local copy — no CDN,\n  offline) and assert no serious/critical violations. Add a Drupal-report render case.\n\n### email (`tests/email/`, mark `email`) — unchanged\n- Stays a single `@pytest.mark.skip` scaffold documenting the future GMail flow.\n\n---\n\n## Fixtures, recording, and determinism\n\n- **Drupal fixtures**: record `its-wws-test2` read-only via `./run-tests --record` extended to\n  the Drupal site (drush metrics/version/module fixtures), reusing `tests/tools/record.py`'s\n  scrub/trim (org list → test site, domain list → platform only, team emails → `test-owner*`).\n  Seed enough months of traffic for the recommendation path; add a second seed for the\n  ≤4-month case.\n- **axe-core**: vendor a pinned `axe.min.js` into `tests/vendor/` (offline; no external host) so\n  the render tier stays hermetic under `--fast`.\n- **Golden normalization**: reuse `normalize_report_html` (CID → `cid:NORMALIZED`); pin\n  `--date 2026-03-31` (mid-year, avoids the June contract-year-end path). Drupal golden uses the\n  same normalization.\n- Recording must never use `--all`/`--for-real`/live `--create-tables`/`--import-older-metrics`.\n\n## Documentation updates (part of the later implementation, specified in SPEC.md)\n\n- **`README.md`** — Testing section: note the Drupal golden, the render tier's a11y/console\n  checks, and the new `--create-tables`/`--import-older-metrics` live-refusal safety rule.\n- **`CLAUDE.md`** — Testing section: the four extracted pure helpers and that they're the unit/\n  property seam; the interlock now also blocks live schema/import flags; that `recommend_plan`\n  is now importable. Keep it to non-obvious-from-code facts only.\n- **`tests/README.md`** — per-tier \"how to add a test\" updated for the new files/fixtures\n  (Drupal golden, plugin mocks, axe vendoring).\n- **`docs/`** — no new end-user docs required (tests are developer-facing); do **not** add\n  internal-mechanics docs to `docs/`.\n- **`prompts/add-tests-for-change.prompt.md`** — already exists and matches; reference it, no\n  rewrite needed.\n\n## Acceptance criteria (each test's \"done\" — enumerated per-test in SPEC.md)\n\n- `./run-tests --fast` is green (offline: unit + integration + e2e + golden + render + property),\n  runnable with no network / no Terminus auth.\n- `./run-tests` (adds `live`) green where live is available; `live` tier never uses forbidden or\n  live-schema flags.\n- `./run-tests --coverage` runs; SPEC.md includes a \"coverage map\" naming intentionally-uncovered\n  paths (the `--all` path, real send, some unguarded U-M branches) so gaps are explicit, not\n  silent. No coverage gate.\n- New interlock tests prove `--create-tables`/`--import-older-metrics` are refused live.\n- Both goldens (WordPress + Drupal) reproduce deterministically; `--update-goldens` is the only\n  sanctioned way to change them.\n\n## Execution steps for THIS session (design only — no tests, no program changes)\n\n1. Write `development/2026-07-04-test-suite/PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md` (full detail of every bug\n   below + investigation notes).\n2. Write `development/2026-07-04-test-suite/SPEC.md` — expand this plan into the implementation-\n   ready spec: per-test acceptance criteria (exact commands + observable outcomes), the required\n   ASCII diagrams (per-site pipeline, mock-seam map, interlock decision tree), the doc-update\n   list, and the \"coverage map\". Optimized for Claude Code to implement later.\n3. Run the adversarial review (independent reviewer subagent; Completeness/Consistency/Clarity/\n   Scope/Feasibility; ≤3 iterations; convergence guard → \"Reviewer Concerns\" section). Report\n   score + issues fixed. If the subagent is unavailable, say \"Spec review unavailable —\n   presenting unreviewed doc.\"\n4. Report results; the user may hand-edit SPEC.md before a future implementation session.\n\n## Discovered problems (summary — full detail goes to PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md)\n\n- **BLOCKING (fix now, Part B):** `median_visitors` / `site_*_plan_index` `NameError` for\n  ≤4-month sites (L3155/L3544–3545/L3555).\n- Dead config-news loop — `[News]` inline items never added (L864–866); only file-based news works.\n- `emails_sent` always 0 but L3676 prints \"Email sent for 0 of N sites\" (increment commented at\n  L3658) — misleading output while SMTP is disabled.\n- `terminus()` silently drops `errors`/`fatal` and returns `\"\"` on JSON-decode failure (L343/\n  L352–353) → `\"\"[\"key\"]` `TypeError` at call sites.\n- DNS exceptions swallowed (L1252–1258, L1282–1288) → domain checks silently skipped.\n- Stale docstring return signatures on `wp`/`wp_eval`/`drush` (declared 2-tuple, return 3-tuple).\n- `plt.close(fig)` comment references non-existent `sc.options.all_sites` (option is `all`, L3666).\n- Institution-specific (U-M) code paths in the core script not behind `[UMich].enabled`\n  (smtp host, several notice URLs, `make_msgid` domain, MIME From/To/Bcc/Reply-to, oidc-login\n  special-case) — latent bugs for non-U-M reuse; catalogue for the future de-monolith stage.\n\n## Verification (of the design artifacts, this session)\n\n- SPEC.md and PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md exist under `development/2026-07-04-test-suite/`.\n- SPEC.md self-consistently references only existing harness fixtures/marks and honors all\n  safety constraints (no `--all`/`--for-real`/live schema flags anywhere).\n- Adversarial review completed (or explicitly reported unavailable) with score + issue log.\n"
}
```
