## Approved Plan (edited by user):
# Plan: Test-suite specification for `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`

## Context

A pytest harness was just built (`development/2026-07-04-test-harness/SPEC.md`) with basic
smoke tests proving the harness works. This task is the **design/specification** step for the
real test suite that will cover the program's existing functionality — so that the upcoming
work (re-enabling SMTP + adding SendGrid, new features, de-monolithing `main()`, moving logic
into the plugin/config frameworks) has a safety net that catches regressions early.

Per the driving prompt (`development/2026-07-04-test-suite/PROMPT.md`), **this session produces
the design artifacts only — it does not implement the tests.** The deliverables of executing
this plan are:

1. `development/2026-07-04-test-suite/SPEC.md` — the complete, implementation-ready test spec
   (the permanent in-repo design record; the user may hand-edit it before implementation).
2. `development/2026-07-04-test-suite/PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md` — program bugs found during
   design, logged for a later fix session (not fixed now, except the one blocking bug below).
3. An adversarial spec-review pass (independent reviewer subagent, ≤3 iterations) with results
   reported back.

Tests, the refactor, and the bug fix described below are **implemented in a later session** from
the approved SPEC.md — not in this one.

The suite must **extend the existing harness and honor its hard safety constraints** — no
parallel testing approach.

## Non-negotiable safety constraints (design-time and every run, now and future)

- **NEVER** `--all` / `-a` (up-to-6-hour full run) and **NEVER** `--for-real` (sends real
  customer email). Already enforced by `run_program()`'s `ForbiddenFlagError` interlock
  (`tests/conftest.py`).
- **NEVER run `--create-tables` or `--import-older-metrics` "live"** (against the real config /
  production MySQL). Only ever against a throwaway temp SQLite DB in offline mode. *New this
  plan* — see Part C.
- Tests use only `its-wws-test1` (WordPress) and `its-wws-test2` (Drupal), read-only.
- No SMTP re-enable, no SMTP tests, no GMail/SendGrid tests — all deferred to a future session.
  The `email` tier stays a skipped scaffold.

## Decisions locked with the user (interview)

| Decision | Choice |
|---|---|
| Refactor for testability | **Extract key pure helpers** from `main()` (behavior-preserving, golden-pinned) |
| Discovered bugs | **Fix only truly-blocking bugs now**, log the rest to PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md |
| Drupal coverage | **Yes** — record `its-wws-test2` fixtures + a second Drupal golden |
| Render tier depth | **Functional + console-error + axe-core a11y smoke** (no pixel screenshots) |
| Plugin tests | **All three**: AWS `get_secret`, Cloudflare `ips`, UMich portal + SiteLens (mock-based) |
| Lower-effort extras | **All four**: MIME/.eml structural, config-substitution engine, argparse contract, Hypothesis property on extracted helpers |
| CI | **No** — local `./run-tests` only |
| Mutation testing | **No** |

## Explicitly NOT in scope (record so it's not silently dropped)

- The `--all` aggregation/CSV/JSON post-loop path (L3674–3695) — unreachable without `--all`.
- Any real SMTP/SendGrid send path; the commented-out `smtp_login()` send.
- GMail rendering/deliverability tests (future session).
- CI workflow, mutation testing, pixel/visual-regression screenshots.
- Full de-monolithing of `main()` — only the four extractions below are pulled forward.
- Live `--create-tables` / `--import-older-metrics`.

---

## Part A — Behavior-preserving extractions (prerequisite for unit/property tests)

Keep the "one big file" convention: define these as **module-level functions in the main
`pantheon-sitehealth-emails` script** (so tests import them as `psh.<fn>`), and call them from
`main()`. Pin behavior with the existing golden e2e (must stay byte-identical after extraction,
modulo the intended bug fix in Part B).

1. **`overage_blocks(overage, block_size) -> int`** — the `round((overage + block/2)/block)`
   rounding used at L3123 and L3165. Pure. High-value boundary tests.
2. **`contract_year_end(report_date) -> bool`** — the "June 16–29" end-of-contract-year check
   (L900–906). Pure. (U-M-specific semantics but harmless/general as a date predicate.)
3. **`estimate_month_visits(...) -> float`** — the current-month traffic extrapolation
   (L2617–2637). Pure given its inputs.
4. **`recommend_plan(...) -> dict`** — the cost model + selection + downgrade guardrails
   (L3105–3295). **Decouple from the DB**: inject overage-protection data as a plain
   `dict[str, OPRecord]` or a `Callable[[str_month], op|None]`, not a live `db_session`.
   Returns a complete result dict: `recommended_plan`, `median_visitors`, `cost_same`,
   `costs_median`, `costs_best`, `current_plan_index`, `recommended_plan_index`,
   `months_until_recommendations`, `cost_table_rows`. **Always returns a complete dict, even
   for ≤4-month sites** (this is where the Part B fix lives).

`main()` changes to call these; the surrounding DB reads (`db_session.get(PantheonOverageProtection, …)`)
are gathered into the injected op-lookup before the call.

## Part B — The one blocking bug fix (folded into the `recommend_plan` extraction)

For sites with ≤4 months of traffic, `main()` builds `template_dict` (L3555, L3544–3545) using
`median_visitors`, `site_current_plan_index`, `site_recommended_plan_index` — all assigned only
inside `if len(v) > 4:` (and, for the indices, only inside the "current != recommended" branch).
Result: `NameError` when rendering any new site. This blocks testing the (valid, common)
new-site path, so it is fixed now.

**Fix:** `recommend_plan` returns sensible defaults for the ≤4-month case — `median_visitors = 0`
(or the mean of available months), indices default to the current plan's index, empty
`cost_table_rows`, `months_until_recommendations = 5 - len(v)`. `main()` reads these off the
returned dict, so the unconditional `template_dict` construction is always well-defined. A new
regression test (`its-wws-test1` with ≤4 months seeded) asserts render succeeds and the template
shows the "not enough data yet" state.

All **other** discovered bugs are logged to PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md and left in place; where a
path is currently broken but not blocking, a **strict-xfail** test documents intended behavior
and auto-alerts when the bug is later fixed.

## Part C — Safety-interlock hardening (`tests/conftest.py`)

Extend `_assert_flags_allowed` / `run_program` so `--create-tables` and `--import-older-metrics`
are **refused whenever the run is not offline** — i.e. blocked in `mode="live"` and blocked
unless the effective `--config` is a test fixture config whose `[Database]` is a temp SQLite
path. Fail-closed with a named exception (extend `ForbiddenFlagError` or add
`ForbiddenLiveDataError`). Add unit tests mirroring `tests/unit/test_interlock.py`. This makes
the "never touch production data" rule structural, not a convention.

---

   below + investigation notes).
2. Write `development/2026-07-04-test-suite/SPEC.md` — expand this plan into the implementation-
   ready spec: per-test acceptance criteria (exact commands + observable outcomes), the required
   ASCII diagrams (per-site pipeline, mock-seam map, interlock decision tree), the doc-update
   list, and the "coverage map". Optimized for Claude Code to implement later.
3. Run the adversarial review (independent reviewer subagent; Completeness/Consistency/Clarity/
   Scope/Feasibility; ≤3 iterations; convergence guard → "Reviewer Concerns" section). Report
   score + issues fixed. If the subagent is unavailable, say "Spec review unavailable —
   presenting unreviewed doc."
4. Report results; the user may hand-edit SPEC.md before a future implementation session.

## Discovered problems (summary — full detail goes to PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md)

- **BLOCKING (fix now, Part B):** `median_visitors` / `site_*_plan_index` `NameError` for
  ≤4-month sites (L3155/L3544–3545/L3555).
- Dead config-news loop — `[News]` inline items never added (L864–866); only file-based news works.
- `emails_sent` always 0 but L3676 prints "Email sent for 0 of N sites" (increment commented at
  L3658) — misleading output while SMTP is disabled.
- `terminus()` silently drops `errors`/`fatal` and returns `""` on JSON-decode failure (L343/
  L352–353) → `""["key"]` `TypeError` at call sites.
- DNS exceptions swallowed (L1252–1258, L1282–1288) → domain checks silently skipped.
- Stale docstring return signatures on `wp`/`wp_eval`/`drush` (declared 2-tuple, return 3-tuple).
- `plt.close(fig)` comment references non-existent `sc.options.all_sites` (option is `all`, L3666).
- Institution-specific (U-M) code paths in the core script not behind `[UMich].enabled`
  (smtp host, several notice URLs, `make_msgid` domain, MIME From/To/Bcc/Reply-to, oidc-login
  special-case) — latent bugs for non-U-M reuse; catalogue for the future de-monolith stage.

## Verification (of the design artifacts, this session)

- SPEC.md and PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md exist under `development/2026-07-04-test-suite/`.
- SPEC.md self-consistently references only existing harness fixtures/marks and honors all
  safety constraints (no `--all`/`--for-real`/live schema flags anywhere).
- Adversarial review completed (or explicitly reported unavailable) with score + issue log.

```
327	def terminus(*args) -> Any:
328	    """
329	    Run Terminus with the given arguments and return the result as a JSON object.
330	    """
331	    # args is a tuple (from *args); work with a list so the retry sentinel can be
332	    # added/removed without mutating a tuple (which previously crashed this path).
333	    args = list(args)
334	    retry = True
335	    if "pshe-no-retry" in args:
336	        args.remove("pshe-no-retry")
337	        retry = False
338	    command = [*args, "--format=json"]
339	    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)
340	    try:
341	        result = json.loads(output)
342	    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
343	        result = ""  # TODO: set to None
344	        errors += "\n" + output + "\n" + str(e)
345	    if errors != "":
346	        sc.console.print(f"[bold red]Terminus error: {errors}")
347	        if retry and "Invalid or expired session header: X-Pantheon-Session" in errors:
348	            sc.console.print("Sleeping for 5 seconds and then retrying...")
349	            time.sleep(5)
350	            args.append("pshe-no-retry")
351	            return terminus(*args)
352	    # return result, errors.strip(), fatal  # TODO
353	    return result
354	
355	
356	def wp(siteenv: str, *args) -> (Any, str):
```

```json
{
  "file_path": "/workspace/development/2026-07-04-test-suite/PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md",
  "content": "# Problems discovered while designing the test suite\n\nLogged during the 2026-07-04 test-suite **design** session (see `PROMPT.md` / `SPEC.md` in this\nfolder). Per the driving prompt, program bugs are **logged here and fixed in a later session**,\n**with one exception**: the single *blocking* bug (P1 below) is fixed as part of test-suite\nimplementation because it makes a valid, common program state (a new site with ≤4 months of\ntraffic) untestable.\n\nLine numbers refer to the working revision at design time (`pantheon-sitehealth-emails`, ~3702\nlines). They will drift; treat them as starting points and re-locate by the described symptom.\n\nAll problems below were found by **reading** the code (plus targeted verification reads). None\nwere reproduced by *running* the program against real sites, because the safety constraints\nforbid `--all` / `--for-real` / live `--create-tables` / live `--import-older-metrics`. Each\nentry notes what still needs to be confirmed at fix time.\n\n---\n\n## P1 — BLOCKING (fixed during test-suite implementation): `NameError` rendering a site with ≤4 months of traffic\n\n**Symptom.** For any site whose traffic history is ≤4 months, `main()` raises\n`NameError: name 'median_visitors' is not defined` (and, on related paths,\n`site_current_plan_index` / `site_recommended_plan_index`) while assembling `template_dict`.\n\n**Root cause.**\n- `median_visitors` is assigned only inside `if len(v) > 4:` at **L3155**.\n- `site_current_plan_index` / `site_recommended_plan_index` are assigned even deeper — inside\n  `if len(v) > 4:` **and** the nested `if site[\"plan_name\"] != site_recommended_plan:` branch\n  (**L3177–3179**).\n- But `template_dict` consumes all three **unconditionally**: `median_monthly_visitors=f\"{median_visitors:,.0f}\"`\n  at **L3555**, and the two indices at **L3544–3545**. This dict is built in Python *before*\n  Jinja sees it, so no template `{% if %}` guard can prevent the `NameError`.\n\n**Why it hasn't blown up in production / existing tests.** The one existing golden\n(`its-wws-test1`) replays recorded metrics that supply >4 months of history, so `len(v) > 4`\nand the variables are defined. Real U-M sites are almost all long-lived. A brand-new site (or\nany site with a short history) hits this. It is also latent cross-iteration state: under `--all`\na prior site's `median_visitors` can leak into a later ≤4-month site, masking the bug\nnon-deterministically.\n\n**Fix (folded into the `recommend_plan(...)` extraction — see SPEC Part A/B).** Have\n`recommend_plan` always return a complete result dict, including for the ≤4-month case:\n`median_visitors = 0` (or mean of available months), `current_plan_index` /\n`recommended_plan_index` defaulting to the current plan's index, empty `cost_table_rows`,\n`months_until_recommendations = 5 - len(v)`. `main()` reads these off the returned dict so\n`template_dict` is always well-defined.\n\n**Verify at fix time.** Offline e2e with `its-wws-test1` seeded with ≤4 months of traffic renders\nwithout error and the template shows the \"not enough data yet\" state; the >4-month golden stays\nbyte-identical (modulo intended output for the new-site case).\n\n---\n\n## P2 — Config-defined `[News]` items are never added (dead loop)\n\n**Symptom.** News items written inline in the config file's `[News]` table never appear in\nreports. Only news loaded from `*.toml` files in `[News].folder` works.\n\n**Root cause (L863–870).**\n```python\nif \"News\" in sc.config:\n    for news_item_name in sc.config[\"News\"].keys():\n        if not isinstance(news_item_name, dict):\n            continue  # skip News configuration directives\n        sc.add_news_item(sc.config[\"News\"][news_item_name], ...)\n```\n`news_item_name` is a **dict key (a string)**, so `isinstance(news_item_name, dict)` is always\n`False` and the `continue` always fires — the `add_news_item` call is unreachable. The guard was\npresumably meant to test the *value* (`sc.config[\"News\"][news_item_name]`) and skip scalar\ndirectives like `folder`.\n\n**Fix (later).** Iterate items and skip non-table values, e.g.\n`for name, value in sc.config[\"News\"].items(): if not isinstance(value, dict): continue`. Confirm\nthe `folder` key (a string) is correctly skipped and only `[News.<x>]` sub-tables are added.\n\n**Test coverage now.** A strict-`xfail` unit/integration test documents the intended behavior\n(config-inline news item shows up) and will flip to passing when fixed. The file-based news path\nis tested normally.\n\n---\n\n## P3 — `terminus()` swallows `errors`/`fatal` and returns `\"\"` on JSON-decode failure\n\n**Root cause (L338–353).** `terminus()` returns **only `result`** (the `return result, errors, fatal`\nline is commented at L352). On a `json.JSONDecodeError` it sets `result = \"\"` (L343, self-marked\n`# TODO: set to None`) and continues. For non-session errors it prints `Terminus error: …`\n(L346) but neither raises, exits, nor signals the caller.\n\n**Consequences.**\n- Callers index directly into the result: `terminus(\"plan:info\", …)[\"sku\"]` (~L972),\n  `terminus(...)[\"timeseries\"]` (~L490/L1081/L1095). When `result == \"\"`, `\"\"[\"sku\"]` raises\n  `TypeError: string indices must be integers` — a crash far from the real cause (a malformed\n  Terminus response), with the original stderr already discarded.\n- Empty-but-valid decode (`result == {}` / `[]`) silently produces zero rows with no signal.\n\n**Fix (later).** Adopt the TODO: return `(result, errors, fatal)` (and `None`, not `\"\"`, on\ndecode failure); update call sites to check `fatal` / `None`. This is entangled with the broader\n\"`terminus()` → return tuple\" item already in the README TODO list.\n\n**Test coverage now.** Integration tests around the `run_terminus` seam pin the *current* return\ncontract (single value) and the session-expiry retry; a strict-`xfail` documents the desired\n`(result, errors, fatal)` contract so the later change is guarded.\n\n---\n\n## P4 — DNS resolution failures are console-only and conflated with \"not in DNS\"\n\n**Root cause (L1252–1259 for A, L1282–1289 for AAAA).** `NoAnswer` / `NXDOMAIN` /\n`NoNameservers` / `Timeout` are each caught and only `sc.console.print(...)`ed. Control then falls\nthrough; `dns_points_at_cloudflare` / `dns_points_elsewhere` remain 0, so L1291 emits\n`ATTENTION: {hostname} is not in DNS` — i.e. a **transient resolver timeout is reported\nidentically to a genuinely-unregistered hostname**, and neither becomes a structured\n`site_context` notice (only console output). Observability gap: the report can't distinguish\n\"DNS is broken right now\" from \"this domain doesn't exist.\"\n\n**Fix (later).** Distinguish transient (`Timeout` / `NoNameservers`) from definitive\n(`NXDOMAIN` / `NoAnswer`) outcomes; surface at least the definitive ones as a report notice via\n`sc.add_notice(...)` rather than console-only.\n\n**Test coverage now.** Not directly tested this round (DNS is stubbed out in offline e2e via\n`fqdns.json = {}` and platform-only `domain:list`). Logged for the later observability pass.\n\n---\n\n## P5 — `emails_sent` counter is dead; `--all` summary line is misleading\n\n**Root cause (L3658, L3676).** `emails_sent += 1` is commented out (SMTP send is disabled), so\nthe counter is never incremented. The only reader is L3676 `f\"Email sent for {emails_sent} of\n{site_count} sites.\"`, inside the `if sc.options.all:` branch.\n\n**Consequences.**\n- The summary always says \"Email sent for 0 of N sites\" even after a successful dry run.\n- If `emails_sent` is not initialized before the loop, L3676 would `NameError` under `--all`\n  (needs confirmation — this path is **out of test scope** because `--all` is forbidden).\n\n**Fix (later, together with SMTP re-enable).** Restore the increment when send is re-enabled and\ninitialize `emails_sent = 0` before the loop; make the dry-run summary count intended-recipients\nrather than sent.\n\n**Test coverage now.** None (lives behind `--all`, which is never run). Logged only.\n\n---\n\n## P6 — Stale docstring return signatures on Terminus wrappers\n\n**Root cause.** `wp()` (L356), `wp_eval()` (L370), and `drush()` (L427) are annotated/documented\nas returning 2-tuples (`-> (Any, str)` / `-> (str, str)`) but actually return **3-tuples**\n`(result, errors, fatal)`; call sites unpack three (e.g. `ocp_config, errors, fatal = wp_eval(...)`\n~L1685). Cosmetic/maintainability, not a runtime bug, but misleads readers and future callers.\n\n**Fix (later).** Correct the annotations/docstrings to the real 3-tuple contract.\n\n**Test coverage now.** Integration `test_wrappers.py` asserts the *actual* 3-tuple shape, which\ndocuments the truth regardless of the stale annotations.\n\n---\n\n## P7 — Misleading comment references a non-existent option\n\n**Root cause (L3666).** `plt.close(fig)  # needed to free up memory when sc.options.all_sites is\nTrue`. The parsed option is `all` (`--all/-a`), not `all_sites`; `sc.options.all_sites` does not\nexist. Comment-only; no runtime effect.\n\n**Fix (later).** Correct the comment to `sc.options.all`.\n\n---\n\n## P8 — Institution-specific (U-M) logic in the core script not behind `[UMich].enabled`\n\n**Not a bug for U-M runs**, but a **reusability defect**: for any non-U-M deployment these paths\neither hardcode U-M specifics or risk `KeyError`. Two in-code comments (≈L3410–3411, L3494–3497)\nalready document that previous `if True:` blocks here crashed non-U-M runs with\n`KeyError('UMich')` and were retrofitted with a guard — evidence the guarding is incomplete.\n\nCatalogue (re-verify lines at fix time) of U-M specifics **not** behind the\n`\"UMich\" in sc.config and sc.config[\"UMich\"][\"enabled\"]` guard:\n- `smtp_login()` — hardcoded `smtp.mail.umich.edu:465` + `SMTP_PASSWORD` (L771).\n- `umich-cloudflare` cache check + `documentation.its.umich.edu/node/5114` (L1569–1577), gated\n  only by `len(fqdns_behind_cloudflare) > 0`.\n- `umich-oidc-login` reinstall special-case (semver, GitHub release URLs, U-M shortcode text)\n  inside the generic plugins loop (L1595–1650).\n- Drupal user-agent check → `documentation.its.umich.edu/node/4242`, `ifconfig.me/ua`\n  (L2093, L2137–2150).\n- Support-URL notice strings `its.umich.edu/computing/web-mobile/pantheon/support`\n  (L1014, L1024) and Cloudflare \"at U-M\" doc URLs (L1429–1471).\n- `make_msgid(domain=\"webservices.umich.edu\")` — unconditional (L3533–3534).\n- MIME headers unconditional (L3607–3617): `From: … <webmaster@umich.edu>`, dry-run `To:` /\n  `Bcc:` `@umich.edu` / `@go.mail.umich.edu`, `Reply-to: webmaster@umich.edu`.\n- Hardcoded site-name special cases `lsa-disko-project`, `umma-inside-wp` (L3390–3392) — inside\n  the guard, but still string-literal site names.\n\n**Fix (later — this is the planned \"move institution logic into plugins/config\" stage).** Move\neach behind `[UMich].enabled` and/or into the `umich` plugin/check packages, or drive from config\n(`[Email].from`, `[Email].reply_to`, doc-URL map, `make_msgid` domain). Add non-U-M-config e2e\ncoverage once guarded.\n\n**Test coverage now.** Not fixed this round. The offline e2e runs *with* U-M behavior baked in\n(the golden reflects it), so these paths are exercised but not proven reusable. A future\nnon-U-M-config golden would prove the guarding.\n\n---\n\n## Non-issues considered and dismissed\n- `terminus()` retry list-mutation (L331–337) — previously a real crash on a `*args` tuple; the\n  code now converts to a list first and is correct. Regression already exists in the harness.\n- `check/umich/__init__.py` `sc.console('…')`-as-callable — already fixed; regression exists.\n"
}

{
  "file_path": "/workspace/development/2026-07-04-test-suite/SPEC.md",
  "content": "# SPEC: Test suite for `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`\n\n**Status:** design, ready to implement. **Do not implement from this file until the owner\napproves it** (they may hand-edit first). This is the permanent in-repo design record for the\ntest-suite work; it is **not** primary documentation of how the program works (that's the code +\n`CLAUDE.md` + `docs/`).\n\nCompanion files in this folder: `PROMPT.md` (the driving request), `PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md`\n(program bugs found during design). Prior work: `../2026-07-04-test-harness/SPEC.md` (the harness\nthis suite extends) and `/workspace/tests/README.md`.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Purpose & guiding principles\n\nThe pytest **harness** exists and its smoke tests pass. This spec defines the **real test\nsuite** that pins the program's *current* behavior, so the upcoming stages — re-enabling SMTP +\nadding SendGrid, new features, de-monolithing `main()`, and moving logic into the plugin/config\nframeworks — have an early-warning net.\n\n- **Pragmatic coverage, not 100%.** Test all meaningful/practical functionality; deliberately\n  leave documented gaps (see §9 Coverage map). Do not chase the coverage metric.\n- **Extend the harness; never fork it.** Reuse its fixtures, marks, mock seams, and the\n  `run_program()` safety interlock. No parallel testing approach.\n- **Tests follow the change (no TDD going forward).** These are the initial characterization\n  tests; future tests land alongside features (see `prompts/add-tests-for-change.prompt.md`).\n- **Robustness over volume.** Prefer tests that survive unrelated edits (behavioral assertions,\n  normalized goldens) over brittle ones (raw string matching, pixel diffs).\n\n## 2. Scope\n\n### In scope\n- Behavior-preserving extraction of four pure helpers from `main()` (§5 Part A).\n- The one blocking bug fix, folded into that extraction (§5 Part B, `PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md` P1).\n- Safety-interlock hardening for `--create-tables` / `--import-older-metrics` (§5 Part C).\n- Test inventory across `unit`, `integration`, `e2e`, `render`, plus Hypothesis property tests,\n  mock-based plugin/check tests, and MIME structural checks (§6).\n- A Drupal (`its-wws-test2`) recorded-fixture path + second golden (§7).\n- Doc updates: `README.md`, `CLAUDE.md`, `tests/README.md` (§10). No new `docs/` files.\n\n### Out of scope (explicit — so nothing is silently dropped)\n- `--all` aggregation/CSV/JSON post-loop path (L3674–3695) — unreachable without `--all`.\n- Any real SMTP/SendGrid send; the commented-out `smtp_login()` send path.\n- GMail rendering/deliverability tests; the `email` tier stays a skipped scaffold.\n- CI, mutation testing, pixel/visual-regression screenshots.\n- Full de-monolithing of `main()` (only the four extractions are pulled forward).\n- **Live `--create-tables` / live `--import-older-metrics`** (production-data risk).\n\n## 3. Hard safety constraints (design-time and every run, forever)\n\n1. **NEVER** `--all` / `-a`; **NEVER** `--for-real`. Enforced by `run_program()` →\n   `ForbiddenFlagError` (`tests/conftest.py`).\n2. **NEVER** run `--create-tables` or `--import-older-metrics` against the real config /\n   production DB. Only against a throwaway temp SQLite DB in offline mode. Enforced structurally\n   by §5 Part C.\n3. Only `its-wws-test1` (WordPress) and `its-wws-test2` (Drupal), read-only.\n4. No SMTP re-enable; no SMTP/SendGrid/GMail tests this round.\n\n## 4. Decisions (locked with owner)\n\n| Decision | Choice |\n|---|---|\n| Refactor for testability | Extract 4 pure helpers, behavior-preserving, golden-pinned |\n| Discovered bugs | Fix only the blocking one (P1) now; log the rest |\n| Drupal coverage | Yes — record `its-wws-test2` + second golden |\n| Render tier depth | Functional + zero-console-error + axe-core a11y smoke (no pixel diffs) |\n| Plugin tests | AWS `get_secret`, Cloudflare `ips`, UMich portal + SiteLens (all mock-based) |\n| Extras | MIME/.eml structural, config-substitution engine, argparse contract, Hypothesis |\n| CI | No (local `./run-tests` only) |\n| Mutation testing | No |\n\n---\n\n## 5. Diagrams\n\n### 5.1 Per-site report pipeline (what the tests exercise)\n\n```\n TOML ─► process_config (pass 1) ─► find_modules(plugin) ─► invoke_hooks(\"setup\")\n   │                                                              │\n   │                                              plugins register substitutions + hooks\n   ▼                                                              ▼\n find_modules(check) ─► process_config (pass 2) ─► DB connect ─► [--create-tables? exit]\n   │                                                              │\n   │                                               news load (config* + files)  (*P2: dead)\n   ▼                                                              ▼\n sites = terminus(\"org:site:list\", org_id) ───────────► FOR each selected site:\n                                                          ├─ metrics fetch → PantheonTraffic upsert (temp DB)\n                                                          ├─ invoke_hooks(\"check\", site_context)  ◄─ SiteLens gauges\n                                                          ├─ domain/DNS/Cloudflare checks (P4)\n                                                          ├─ WP/Drupal plugin/module checks\n                                                          ├─ traffic aggregate ─► recommend_plan(...)  ◄─ EXTRACTED (A/B)\n                                                          ├─ surge bar chart (matplotlib → chart_cid)\n                                                          ├─ render Jinja html+txt → build/<site>.{html,txt}\n                                                          ├─ inline-styles.php (real PHP) → *-inline2.html\n                                                          └─ MIME assemble → build/<site>.eml   ◄─ MIME test (§6)\n                                                          (SMTP send: DISABLED / commented)\n```\n\n### 5.2 Mock-seam map (how each tier intercepts I/O)\n\n```\n layer                unit          integration        e2e (offline)     live\n ───────────────────  ───────────   ────────────────   ───────────────   ──────────────\n Pantheon/WP/Drush    call helper   monkeypatch        PATH-shim fake    real terminus\n   (run_terminus)     directly      run_terminus/      terminus          (read-only,\n                                    terminus           (replay JSON)     test sites only)\n Database             n/a           temp_db (sqlite)   temp sqlite       real config DB\n                                                       (minimal.toml)    → NEVER schema/import\n CSS inliner          n/a           n/a                real php          real php\n (inline-styles.php)\n Browser render       n/a           n/a                Playwright        (n/a)\n AWS / Cloudflare /   mock client   mock client /      disabled in       (not exercised)\n   portal DB          (stub)        temp sqlite        minimal.toml\n```\n\n### 5.3 Interlock decision tree (`run_program` / `_assert_flags_allowed`)\n\n```\n run_program(args, mode)\n   │\n   ├─ any of {--all, -a, --for-real} (incl. = -forms, abbrevs, bundled -a)? ─► raise ForbiddenFlagError\n   │\n   ├─ any of {--create-tables, --import-older-metrics}?\n   │      │\n   │      ├─ mode == \"live\"?                       ─► raise ForbiddenLiveDataError\n   │      └─ --config not a temp/fixture sqlite?   ─► raise ForbiddenLiveDataError\n   │\n   └─ otherwise ─► exec program\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Part A — Behavior-preserving extractions\n\nDefine these as **module-level functions in the main `pantheon-sitehealth-emails` script**\n(preserve the \"one big file\" convention; do **not** create a new module). Tests import them as\n`psh.<fn>`. `main()` is edited to call them. The existing >4-month golden must stay\nbyte-identical after extraction (the only intended output change is the new ≤4-month path, P1).\n\n| Fn | Source range | Signature (proposed) | Purity |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `overage_blocks` | L3123–3125, L3165 | `overage_blocks(overage: float, block_size: float) -> int` | pure |\n| `contract_year_end` | L900–906 | `contract_year_end(report_date: datetime.date) -> bool` | pure |\n| `estimate_month_visits` | L2617–2637 | `estimate_month_visits(...) -> float` (finalize args from the block: partial-month visits, day-of-month, days-in-month) | pure |\n| `recommend_plan` | L3105–3295 | see below | pure once DB is injected |\n\n**`recommend_plan` contract.**\n```\nrecommend_plan(\n    plan_info: dict,               # config [Pantheon.plan_info]\n    plan_names: list[str],         # ordered cheapest→most expensive\n    current_plan_name: str,\n    visits_by_month: dict[str,int],# \"YYYY-MM\" -> visits\n    estimate: float,               # current-month projection (0 if none)\n    end_date_yyyy_mm: str,\n    site_plan_start,               # date\n    overage_block_size: float,\n    overage_block_cost: float,\n    op_lookup: Callable[[str], OP|None] | dict[str, OP],  # month \"YYYY-MM\" -> PantheonOverageProtection|None\n) -> dict  # keys: recommended_plan, median_visitors, cost_same, costs_median, costs_best,\n           #       current_plan_index, recommended_plan_index, months_until_recommendations,\n           #       cost_table_rows\n```\n`main()` gathers the `PantheonOverageProtection` rows it needs (currently `db_session.get(...)`\ninside the loop, L3128–3134) into `op_lookup` **before** calling, so the function is DB-free and\nunit-testable. Keep the conservative selection (`costs_best = max(cost_same, costs_median)`;\n`recommended = min(costs_best)`) and the downgrade guardrails (Basic special-case, \"Performance\nSmall\" floor, intermediate-plan search) exactly as-is.\n\n**Acceptance (Part A).**\n- `./run-tests --fast` green.\n- `./run-tests -m e2e` golden unchanged for the >4-month `its-wws-test1` case\n  (`git diff tests/e2e/__snapshots__/test_golden.ambr` empty).\n- `python -c \"import importlib.util,...; psh.recommend_plan\"` importable (covered by the unit\n  tests below actually calling it).\n\n## 6b. Part B — Blocking bug fix (folded into `recommend_plan`)\n\n`recommend_plan` returns a **complete dict even when `len(visits) ≤ 4`**: `median_visitors = 0`\n(or mean of available months — pick one and pin it in the test), `current_plan_index =\nrecommended_plan_index = plan_names.index(current_plan_name)`, `cost_same = costs_median =\ncosts_best = {}`, `cost_table_rows = {}`, `months_until_recommendations = 5 - len(visits)`,\n`recommended_plan = current_plan_name`. `main()` reads these instead of the current inline\nlocals, eliminating the `NameError` (`PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md` P1).\n\n**Acceptance (Part B).** New e2e case: `its-wws-test1` seeded with ≤4 months renders with exit 0\nand the HTML contains the \"not enough data yet\" state (assert on the\n`months_until_recommendations`-driven copy in `email_template.html`); no `NameError` in stderr.\n\n## 6c. Part C — Interlock hardening (`tests/conftest.py`)\n\n- Add `class ForbiddenLiveDataError(RuntimeError)` (named; fail-closed) exported like\n  `ForbiddenFlagError`.\n- In `_assert_flags_allowed` (or a sibling `_assert_offline_data_flags`), detect\n  `--create-tables` / `--import-older-metrics` (exact, `=`-form, and abbrev-prefix forms, mirror\n  the existing `_FORBIDDEN_LONG` logic). If present and either `mode == \"live\"` **or** the\n  resolved `--config` is not a known temp/fixture SQLite config → raise `ForbiddenLiveDataError`.\n- `run_program(...)` calls it for every invocation.\n- Add a `forbidden_live_data_error` fixture returning the class (mirrors\n  `forbidden_flag_error`, avoids the double-import identity trap).\n\n**Acceptance (Part C).** Parametrized `tests/unit/test_interlock.py` cases:\n`--create-tables` / `--import-older-metrics` (and `--create` / `--import` abbrev forms) with\n`mode=\"live\"` raise `ForbiddenLiveDataError`; the same flags in offline mode with the minimal\nfixture config do **not** raise. `./run-tests -m unit -k interlock` green.\n\n---\n\n## 7. Test inventory (per file, per test, with acceptance criteria)\n\nConventions for every test: `pytestmark = pytest.mark.<tier>` at module top; reuse fixtures\n`psh`, `reset_sc`, `temp_db`, `program_runner`/`run_program`, `rendered_report`, `normalize_html`,\n`forbidden_flag_error`, `forbidden_live_data_error`; import constants `from conftest import …`.\n\"Done\" = the stated command passes and the stated observable holds.\n\n### 7.1 unit — pure, in-process (`tests/unit/`, mark `unit`)\n\n**`test_plan_math.py`**\n- `overage_blocks`: `(0, 10000) == 0`; `(10000, 10000) == 1`; half-block rounding both directions\n  (`(4999,10000)==1` and `(5000,10000)==1` per `round(half)` banker's rounding — pin the actual\n  observed value, don't assume); large overage scales linearly.\n- `contract_year_end`: `date(2026,6,16)`→True … `date(2026,6,29)`→True; `6/15` and `6/30`→False;\n  any non-June date→False. (Confirm the exact inclusive bounds against L900–906 at implement time.)\n- `estimate_month_visits`: mid-month partial → proportional projection; day 1 and last-day edges.\n- **Acceptance:** `./run-tests -m unit -k plan_math` green.\n\n**`test_recommend_plan.py`** — parametrized over crafted `plan_info` (use the minimal fixture's\ntables) + synthetic `visits_by_month` + an in-memory `op_lookup` dict:\n- All months below every `traffic_limit` → recommends the cheapest adequate plan.\n- Sustained overage beyond current plan → recommends an upgrade.\n- `op_lookup` returning a `used_this_month=True` record → that month's overage cost zeroed.\n- Retroactive OP (no record, month endswith `-01`) → 4-month waiver window applied.\n- Downgrade guardrails: never below \"Performance Small\" via the median path; Basic special-case;\n  intermediate-plan search excludes Basic.\n- ≤4-month input → the P1 default dict (recommended == current, `median_visitors == 0`,\n  `months_until_recommendations == 5 - len`).\n- **Acceptance:** `./run-tests -m unit -k recommend_plan` green; every branch above has ≥1 case.\n\n**`test_config_substitution.py`** — feed synthetic `sc.substitutions`:\n- `<{ secret aws foo bar }>`-style resolves to the registered func's return.\n- `shlex` tokenizing (quoted args with spaces); `$`-wildcard scoring picks the most-specific match.\n- Two-pass semantics: a substitution registered during a (simulated) setup hook resolves on the\n  second `process_config` pass but not the first.\n- Unknown expr / no match / func returns `None` → `pytest.raises(SystemExit)`.\n- **Acceptance:** `./run-tests -m unit -k config_substitution` green.\n\n**`test_argparse_contract.py`** — `psh.build_arg_parser()` / `psh.parse_args`:\n- `--create-tables` + `--import-older-metrics` together → parser/`main` rejects (assert the\n  actual mechanism: if argparse mutual-exclusion, `SystemExit`; if checked in `main`, test via\n  `run_program` expecting nonzero exit — pick per the code at L797–807).\n- Neither sites nor `--all` → rejected (offline, via `run_program`, nonzero exit + message).\n- `--date 2026-13-40` → `SystemExit` (fromisoformat failure); `--date 2026-03-31` parses to\n  `datetime.date`.\n- `allow_abbrev=False`: `--fo`, `--al` → `SystemExit` (unknown option).\n- Defaults: `--smtp-username` falls back to `$USER`; `--config` default filename; `-vvv` →\n  `verbose == 3`.\n- **Acceptance:** `./run-tests -m unit -k argparse` green.\n\n**`test_interlock.py`** (extend) — add Part C cases (§6c). **Acceptance:** as §6c.\n\n**`test_pure_functions.py`, `test_property.py`** (existing) — keep `escape_url`, `fix_drush_output`.\n\n### 7.2 property — Hypothesis (`tests/unit/test_property_plan.py`, mark `unit`)\n- `overage_blocks`: `@given` non-negative floats — result is a non-negative int, non-decreasing in\n  `overage`, and `overage == 0 → 0`.\n- `recommend_plan`: `@given` 0…N months of arbitrary non-negative visits — never raises; returns a\n  `recommended_plan ∈ plan_names`; `costs_best[p] == max(cost_same[p], costs_median[p])` for all p\n  in the >4-month case; recommended has the min `costs_best`.\n- **Acceptance:** `./run-tests -m unit -k property` green (Hypothesis default example budget).\n\n### 7.3 integration (`tests/integration/`, mark `integration`) — monkeypatch `run_terminus`, `temp_db`\n\n**`test_wrappers.py`**\n- `terminus()` session-expiry retry: monkeypatch `run_terminus` to return the expired-session\n  error once then success; monkeypatch `psh.time.sleep`; assert exactly one retry and final\n  success (mirror existing regression idiom).\n- `terminus()` JSON-decode failure → returns `\"\"` (pins current contract, P3); add a\n  **strict-xfail** asserting the desired `(result, errors, fatal)` contract.\n- `wp`/`wp_eval`/`drush`/`drush_php_script` return `(result, errors, fatal)` 3-tuples (documents\n  reality vs the stale docstrings, P6).\n- `wp_error`/`drush_error` produce the expected notice dict-list shape (html+text+csv keys).\n- **Acceptance:** `./run-tests -m integration -k wrappers` green.\n\n**`test_db_roundtrip.py`** — `temp_db`:\n- `PantheonTraffic` merge/upsert is idempotent (same `(site_id, traffic_date)` re-merged updates,\n  doesn't duplicate); unique constraint holds.\n- `PantheonOverageProtection` get/add/update on `(site_id, month)`.\n- **Acceptance:** `./run-tests -m integration -k db_roundtrip` green.\n\n**`test_mime_structure.py`** — parse `rendered_report['eml']` with `email.parser`:\n- Top level `multipart/alternative` with a non-empty `text/plain` part and an HTML part.\n- HTML part carries `related` images; **every `cid:` in the HTML has a matching `Content-ID`\n  related part and every related part is referenced** (bidirectional integrity).\n- `From`/`To`/`Subject` headers present; dry-run `To` is the logged-in user (not an owner).\n- **Acceptance:** `./run-tests -m integration -k mime` green.\n\n### 7.4 plugin/check tests (`tests/integration/`, mark `integration`) — mock-based, no live calls\n\n**`test_plugin_aws.py`** — `botocore.Stubber` (or `moto`) around the boto3 Secrets Manager client:\n- `get_secret(name, key)` returns the parsed JSON value; `SecretString` and base64 `SecretBinary`\n  both decode; second call hits the module cache (stub asserts one API call); missing key →\n  `KeyError`. Load `plugin/aws/get_secret.py` in isolation (its own `SourceFileLoader`, like\n  `test_regressions.py`) with a minimal `sc.config['AWS']`.\n- **Acceptance:** `./run-tests -m integration -k plugin_aws` green.\n\n**`test_plugin_cloudflare.py`** — mock the `Cloudflare` client (`ips.list()` returns synthetic\nCIDR lists):\n- v4/v6 CIDR strings become `ipaddress.ip_network` objects stored in `sc.plugin_context`.\n- Client raising → `pytest.raises(SystemExit)` (the `sys.exit('ERROR: Unable to get lists…')`).\n- **Acceptance:** `./run-tests -m integration -k plugin_cloudflare` green.\n\n**`test_plugin_umich_portal.py`** — temp SQLite engine standing in for the portal MySQL DB:\ncreate `sites_site` / `sites_pantheonplan` tables, insert rows, monkeypatch the plugin's engine\ncreation to point at the temp engine:\n- `plan_sku_to_name` in `sc.config` is overridden from `sites_pantheonplan`.\n- `sc.config['UMich']['portal']['sites']` populated keyed by `site_slug`.\n- Hook ordering: `setup` fires `setup_portal_db`, which fires `setup.umich.portal` (SiteLens\n  setup) before the per-site `check` hooks.\n- **Acceptance:** `./run-tests -m integration -k umich_portal` green.\n\n**`test_check_sitelens.py`**:\n- Gauge color thresholds (pure): `>=90 → GOOD (#00CC66)`, `>=50 → OK (#FFAA33)`, else red\n  (`#FF3333`) — test the boundary values 89/90 and 49/50.\n- `check_sitelens_scores(site_context)` with mocked `sitelens_scores` adds a \"SiteLens\" section\n  and one inline PNG attachment per score with a `cid` and `disposition:'inline'`.\n- `check_sitelens_urls(site_context)` with <4 configured paths adds the \"add paths\" info notice.\n- **Acceptance:** `./run-tests -m integration -k sitelens` green.\n\n### 7.5 e2e (`tests/e2e/`, mark `e2e`) — shim/replay, offline, temp SQLite\n\n**`test_shim_e2e.py`, `test_golden.py`** (existing WordPress) — keep. **Add** to `test_golden.py`\n(or a new `test_golden_newsite.py`) the **≤4-month** case (Part B) with its own seed and, if the\ncopy differs enough, its own snapshot.\n\n**`test_golden_drupal.py`** + `tests/e2e/__snapshots__/test_golden_drupal.ambr` — Drupal golden\nfor mark `render`) — Playwright, skips if no Chromium\nRework the existing test (keep the graceful skip-with-hint if Chromium can't launch):\n- Rewrite `cid:` image sources in the rendered HTML to `data:` URIs (from the `.eml` related\n  parts) so images actually load; load via `sync_playwright`.\n- Assert **zero console errors** (collect `page.on(\"console\")`, fail on `error`-level).\n- Assert Fixtures, recording, determinism\n\n- **Drupal recording:** extend `tests/tools/record.py` (or add a sibling entry) so\n  `./run-tests --record` also records `its-wws-test2` read-only, reusing the existing scrub/trim\n  (org list → test site; `domain:list` → `type==\"platform\"` only, so replay makes no live DNS;\n  team emails → `test-owner{1,2}@umich.edu`). Coverage map (intentionally uncovered — gaps are explicit, not silent)\n\nRun `./run-tests --coverage` (measured, **no gate**). Known-and-accepted uncovered regions:\n- `--all` aggregation + CSV/JSON output (L3674–3695) — forbidden flag.\n- Real SMTP/SendGrid send + `smtp_login()` (commented) — deferred.\n- Live `--create-tables` / `--import-older-metrics` — forbidden by §6c.\n- DNS-failure branches (L1252–1289) — stubbed offline; logged as P4.\n- Some U-M-only branches proven present but not proven reusable (P8) until a non-U-M golden exists.\n- Coverage is measured for in-process tiers only (subprocess e2e not counted without\n  `COVERAGE_PROCESS_START` plumbing, which is out of scope).\n\nImplementation must **`log`/note these** in the coverage summary or `tests/README.md` so a reader\ndoesn't mistake the gaps for \"everything covered.\"\n\n## 10. Documentation updates (part of implementation)\n\n- **`README.md`** Testing section: Drupal golden; render tier does console-error + axe a11y\n  smoke; new live-refusal rule for `--create-tables`/`--import-older-metrics`.\n- **`CLAUDE.md`** Testing section (non-obvious-only): the four extracted pure helpers are the\n  unit/property seam and `recommend_plan` is importable; the interlock now also blocks live\n  schema/import flags (`ForbiddenLiveDataError`); the ≤4-month path is now defined (P1 fixed).\n- **`tests/README.md`**: per-tier \"how to add a test\" for the new files, the Drupal golden, the\n  plugin mocks, `seed_traffic_short`, and the vendored axe version.\n- **`docs/`**: none (developer-facing; `docs/` is end-user only).\n- **`prompts/add-tests-for-change.prompt.md`**: already matches; no change.\n\n## 11. Global acceptance criteria\n\n1. `./run-tests --fast` green offline (no network, no Terminus auth): unit + integration + e2e +\n   golden + render (or skip) + property.\n2. `./run-tests` green where live is available; the `live` tier uses no forbidden flag and no live\n   schema/import flag.\n3. `./run-tests --coverage` runs and the coverage map (§9) is reflected in output/`tests/README.md`.\n4. Interlock: `--create-tables`/`--import-older-metrics` refused live (new tests prove it);\n   `--all`/`-a`/`--for-real` still refused.\n5. Both goldens reproduce byte-for-byte; the >4-month WordPress golden is unchanged by the Part A\n   extraction; changes only via `--update-goldens`.\n6. `PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md` P1 fixed (new-site renders); P2/P3/P6 have strict-xfail guards; the\n   rest logged.\n7. `git status` shows only intended new/edited files; no stray `build/`, `database.db`, `.eml`.\n\n## 12. ```
Verification complete. All load-bearing claims checked against source. Findings below.

---

**1. Completeness** — PASS (with one minor gap)
Tiers, edge cases, and acceptance criteria are thorough (unit/property/integration/plugin/e2e/render/email all covered; P1 fix, interlock hardening, Drupal golden, coverage map all present). Minor: §6 extracts `estimate_month_visits` but its source range L2617–2637 over-includes the `estimates_by_month` chart-array build (L2634–2638), which is plotting data, not part of the scalar estimate (actual pure logic is L2617–2633). Fix: narrow the cited extraction range to L2617–2633 so the implementer doesn't drag chart state into a "pure" helper.

**2. Consistency** — ISSUES
- Verified TRUE: P1 `NameError` — `median_visitors` assigned only at L3155 inside `if len(v) > 4:`; consumed unconditionally at L3555 (`median_monthly_visitors=f"{median_visitors:,.0f}"`) and indices at L3544–3545. Confirmed.
- Verified TRUE: P2 dead news loop — L863–866, `isinstance(news_item_name, dict)` on a dict *key* (string) is always False, `continue` always fires. Confirmed.
- Verified TRUE: `recommend_plan` range L3105–3295, `costs_best = max(cost_same, costs_median)` at L3173, `min(costs_best)` at L3175, Basic/Performance-Small guardrails L3186–3195. Confirmed. `op_lookup` DB call at L3128–3134 confirmed (keyed on site_id + `date.fromisoformat(month+"-01")`).
- Verified TRUE: `contract_year_end` = `end_date.month == 6 and 16 <= end_date.day < 30` (L903–905); §7.1's 6/16→True … 6/29→True, 6/15 & 6/30→False is correct.
- **WRONG assertion**: §7.1 `test_plan_math` states `overage_blocks(10000, 10000) == 1`. The behavior-preserving formula (L3123–3125) is `round((overage + block/2)/block)`; I ran it: `round(1.5) == 2` (banker's rounding), so the true value is **2, not 1**. This concrete example contradicts both the source and the section's own "banker's rounding" note. Fix: change the example to `(10000,10000) == 2`, or drop the hard-coded value and rely on the "pin the observed value" instruction.
- Minor: §6 cites `contract_year_end` source as L900–906, but L900–902 is the unrelated `start_date` computation; the function is only L903–905. Tighten the range.

**3. Clarity** — ISSUES
- §6c defines the live-data trigger as "`--config` is not a known temp/fixture SQLite config" but never defines how the interlock recognizes one. "Known temp/fixture" must be spelled out (see Feasibility below) — as written a competent engineer cannot implement `_assert_offline_data_flags` without guessing the criterion.
- §6b offers `median_visitors = 0` "(or mean of available months — pick one)", but §7.1/§7.4 both hard-assert `== 0`. The optionality is dead and mildly contradictory; state flatly "use 0" so the contract and tests agree.
- `recommend_plan` contract documents `estimate: float # (0 if none)`, but the codebase's sentinel is **-1** (L2617, checked via `estimate > 0` internally and `estimate >= 0` for template display at L3553). An implementer who normalizes -1→0 per this note would flip the template's `current_month_estimate` from "" to "Estimate … 0" and **break the golden**. Reconcile: state that the no-estimate sentinel stays -1 and lives in `main()`, and `recommend_plan` only relies on `> 0`.

**4. Scope** — PASS
No creep. Out-of-scope list (§2) is explicit; hard safety constraints (§3) hold. All tests use only its-wws-test1/test2 read-only; no test invokes `--all`/`--for-real`; §6c/§7.4 exercise `--create-tables`/`--import-older-metrics` only offline against the fixture config; SMTP/SendGrid/GMail deferred (§7.7 skip scaffold). Recording (§8) trims to the test site and forbids live schema/import. Nothing violates the interlock.

**5. Feasibility** — ISSUES
- **Extraction name-shadow trap (concrete bug the SPEC will cause):** `recommend_plan` already contains a *local* named `overage_blocks` (L3123). If the extracted module-level function is also named `overage_blocks` and `recommend_plan` is refactored to call it, Python treats `overage_blocks` as a local throughout the function → the call site raises `UnboundLocalError`. The SPEC must instruct renaming the local (e.g. `n_blocks = overage_blocks(...)`) at L3123 and L3165. Not currently noted anywhere.
- **Interlock cannot distinguish fixture-sqlite from the live config by "is it sqlite" — fail-open risk.** CLAUDE.md/architecture: the production default `[Database]` backend *is* sqlite (`database.db` in repo). So a rule of the form "raise unless config is sqlite" (as the §5.3 decision tree "`--config` not a temp/fixture sqlite? → raise" reads) would **let live `--create-tables` through against the default production config**. The criterion must be an explicit allowlist of resolved fixture config paths (realpath under `tests/fixtures/config/` or the tmp workdir), not a backend-type test. This is the one safety-relevant defect; call it out explicitly in §6c and redraw the §5.3 leaf as "config not in the fixture-path allowlist → raise."
- Byte-identical golden after extraction: feasible provided purity is preserved (np.float64 formatting is identical) — but hinges on the two items above not altering values.
- Decoupling via `op_lookup`, vendoring axe offline, and the umich portal temp-SQLite substitution are all feasible; §13 already flags the portal engine-injection seam. Good.

---

QUALITY SCORE: 7/10
VERDICT: ISSUES
1. [Consistency] §7.1 asserts `overage_blocks(10000,10000)==1`; actual behavior-preserving value is `2` (banker's rounding of 1.5) — fix the example to `==2` or remove the hard-coded value.
2. [Feasibility] Extracting a module-level `overage_blocks` collides with the same-named local at L3123 inside `recommend_plan`, causing `UnboundLocalError` — instruct renaming the local (e.g. `n_blocks`) at L3123 and L3165.
3. [Feasibility/Clarity] §6c/§5.3 interlock keys "live vs test" on sqlite-ness, but the production default config is also sqlite → live `--create-tables` could pass — redefine the check as an explicit allowlist of resolved fixture config paths and specify it in §6c.
4. [Clarity] `recommend_plan` contract says `estimate` is "0 if none" while the code sentinel is -1 (template uses `estimate >= 0`); normalizing to 0 would break the golden — state the sentinel stays -1 in `main()`.
5. [Clarity] §6b's "0 (or mean of available months)" optionality contradicts the `==0` assertions in §7.1/§7.4 — commit to `median_visitors = 0`.
6. [Completeness/Consistency] Tighten cited source ranges: `estimate_month_visits` to L2617–2633 (exclude chart-array build) and `contract_year_end` to L903–905 (exclude `start_date`).

## Assistant

Design complete. Here's the outcome.

## Result

Your spec survived **2 rounds** of adversarial review. **6 issues caught and fixed. Quality score: 9/10 (PASS).**

Two deliverables written to `development/2026-07-04-test-suite/`:
- **`SPEC.md`** — implementation-ready test spec (pipeline/mock-seam/interlock diagrams, per-test acceptance criteria, coverage map, doc-update list, QC self-scores).
- **`PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md`** — 8 logged program bugs (P1 blocking → fix during impl; P2–P8 deferred).

## What the review caught and I fixed

The reviewer independently re-verified my load-bearing code claims against source (P1 `NameError`, dead news loop, `recommend_plan` range, `contract_year_end` bounds) — all confirmed. It then found six real defects, two of them serious:

1. **Interlock fail-open (safety).** My draft keyed "test vs live" on SQLite-ness — but the program's *production default* DB is also SQLite (`database.db`), so live `--create-tables` would have slipped through. Rewrote §5.3/§6c to use a `realpath` **fixture-path allowlist**, explicitly not a backend-type check.
2. **`overage_blocks` name-shadow.** `recommend_plan` binds a local named `overage_blocks`; extracting a module-level helper of the same name → `UnboundLocalError` at runtime. Added an "Extraction gotchas" note instructing the local be renamed (`n_blocks`).
3. **Wrong pinned value** — `overage_blocks(10000,10000)` is `2`, not `1` (banker's rounding of `1.5`). Corrected the example set.
4. **`estimate` sentinel** is `-1`, not `0`; normalizing it inside `recommend_plan` would break the golden. Pinned the contract to leave the sentinel in `main()`.
5. Committed `median_visitors = 0` (removed the ambiguous "or mean") to match the test assertions.
6. Tightened cited source ranges (`estimate_month_visits` L2617–2633; `contract_year_end` L903–905).

Reviewer's only remaining note is cosmetic (no defect). No new issues introduced.

## Spine of the plan (as approved)
Extract 4 pure helpers from `main()` (golden-pinned) → fold the P1 fix into `recommend_plan` → harden the interlock against live schema/import flags → test inventory across unit/property/integration/plugin/e2e/render, WordPress **+ Drupal** goldens, functional+console+axe render tier. Safety constraints (`--all`/`--for-real`, live `--create-tables`/`--import-older-metrics`, test sites only, SMTP/GMail deferred) are enforced throughout.

Per your prompt, **nothing was implemented** — no tests written, no program code changed. `SPEC.md` is yours to hand-edit; when you're ready, point me at it and I'll implement (starting with the P1 fix + extractions, then the tiers, keeping `./run-tests --fast` green).

One flag worth your attention: `PROBLEMS-DISCOVERED.md` **P8** catalogs the U-M-specific code still not behind `[UMich].enabled` — that's the raw material for your later "move institution logic into plugins/config" stage, and a non-U-M golden is the test that would prove it reusable.

## Assistant

Stop — I've found something that overturns a load-bearing part of the approved spec, and I won't build on a false premise without flagging it.

**Finding 1 — the "blocking bug" P1 does not actually exist.** I re-read the initializers I'd missed during design:
- L985–988 initialize `site_current_plan`, `site_recommended_plan`, `site_current_plan_index = 0`, **`site_recommended_plan_index = 0`**.
- L3097 initializes `median_visitors = 0` (plus `cost_same`, `costs_median`, `cost_table_rows`).

Every variable `template_dict` consumes is initialized *before* the `if len(v) > 4:` block, so a ≤4-month (new) site renders fine — there is **no `NameError`**. My design-time verification read the assignments *inside* the guarded block and the unconditional template usage, but didn't scroll up to the early defaults. So there's no blocking bug to fix, and the user decision "fix blocking bugs now" is moot.

**Finding 2 — `recommend_plan` isn't cleanly extractable as specced.** The block at L3175–3295 is interwoven with `main()` side effects: it appends to `site_notices`/`site_savings`, builds U-M portal-URL "before June 30" messaging, and sets `extra_message`/`extra_text` consumed downstream. A pure `recommend_plan` returning that whole dict would drag U-M-specific messaging into a "pure" function — which the SPEC itself says belongs to the later de-monolith stage. The cleanly-pure part is the **cost model** (L3110–3175: `cost_same`/`costs_median`/`costs_best`/`median_visitors`).

Both change what "implement everything" should mean, so I need your calls before proceeding.

753	def find_modules(module_type: str) -> list[str]:
754	    modules = []
755	    # find all non-empty regular files in/under the directory f"{type}" that are named "__init__.py":
756	    for dirpath, dirs, files in os.walk(module_type, followlinks=True):
757	        for file in files:
758	            if file == "__init__.py":
759	                target = os.path.join(dirpath, file)
760	                st = os.stat(target)
761	                if stat.S_ISREG(st.st_mode) and st.st_size != 0:
762	                    parts = target.split("/")[:-1]
763	                    target_name = ".".join(parts)
764	                    modules.append(target_name)
765	    modules.sort()  # ensure a consistent order when importing to simplify troubleshooting
766	    return modules

### ↳ Tool result

```
247	# ── The one sanctioned way to run the program ───────────────────────────────────────
248	# The dangerous long options whose argparse abbreviations must also be blocked.
249	_FORBIDDEN_LONG = ("--all", "--for-real")
250	
251	
252	def _forbidden_msg(token):
253	    return (
254	        f"refusing to run the program with {token!r}: it maps to a forbidden option "
255	        "(constraints C1/C2: never --all/-a/--for-real, incl. abbreviations and short bundles)"
256	    )
257	
258	
259	def _assert_flags_allowed(args):
260	    """Fail closed if any arg could activate --all/-a/--for-real.
261	
262	    Exact-token matching is not enough: the program's argparse accepts abbreviations
263	    (--fo -> --for-real, --al -> --all) and short-flag bundles (-av -> -a -v). This checks
264	    all three forms. It is deliberately conservative (fail-closed) on ambiguous short bundles.
265	    """
266	    for arg in args:
267	        if arg == "--":
268	            break  # everything after "--" is positional, never an option
269	        token = arg.split("=", 1)[0]
270	        if token in FORBIDDEN_FLAGS:
271	            raise ForbiddenFlagError(_forbidden_msg(token))
272	        # A long-option that is a prefix of a forbidden long flag (argparse abbreviation).
273	        if token.startswith("--") and len(token) > 2 and any(
274	            forbidden.startswith(token) for forbidden in _FORBIDDEN_LONG
275	        ):
276	            raise ForbiddenFlagError(_forbidden_msg(token))
277	        # A bundled short flag that includes -a, e.g. "-av" == "-a -v".
278	        if len(token) > 1 and token[0] == "-" and token[1] != "-" and "a" in token[1:]:
279	            raise ForbiddenFlagError(_forbidden_msg(token))
280	
281	
282	def run_program(args, *, cwd, mode="replay", extra_env=None, timeout=300):
283	    """Run ./pantheon-sitehealth-emails as a subprocess through the terminus shim.

```
667	def config_substitution(expr: str, path) -> str:
668	    argv = list(shlex.shlex(expr, posix=True))
669	    argc = len(argv)
670	    if sc.options.verbose > 1:
671	        sc.debug(f"\nconfig_substitution: {path}")
672	        pprint(argv)
673	    if argc == 0:
674	        return ""
675	
676	    # Figure out which substitution matches the expression most closely:
677	    best_match = None
678	    best_match_score = 0
679	    best_match_args_map = {}
680	    for match in sc.substitutions:
681	        match_args = match["args"]
682	        match_args_len = len(match_args)
683	        match_score = 0
684	        args_map = {}
685	        for i in range(argc):
686	            if i >= match_args_len:
687	                break
688	            if match_args[i] == argv[i]:
689	                match_score += 1
690	            elif match_args[i].startswith("$"):
691	                match_score += 1
692	                args_map[match_args[i]] = argv[i]
693	            else:
694	                break
695	        if match_score > best_match_score:
696	            best_match = match
697	            best_match_score = match_score
698	            best_match_args_map = args_map
699	            if match_score == argc and match_score == match_args_len:
700	                break
701	
702	    if sc.options.verbose >= 2:
703	        sc.debug(f"best_match: {best_match_score}")
704	        pprint(best_match_args_map)
705	        pprint(best_match)
706	
707	    if best_match_score == argc:
708	        func_args = [best_match_args_map[arg] for arg in best_match["func_args"]]
709	        if sc.options.verbose >= 2:
710	            sc.debug("args:")
711	            pprint(func_args)
712	        result = best_match["func"](*func_args)
713	        if result is None:
714	            sys.exit(1)
715	        return str(result)
716	
717	    if best_match_score == 0:
718	        sc.console.print(
719	            f"[bold red]ERROR: configuration file value for {path} contains an unknown substitution: {expr}"
720	        )
721	        sys.exit(1)
722	
723	    sc.console.print(
724	        f"[bold red]ERROR: no match found for configuration file value of {path}"
725	    )
726	    sc.console.print(f"[bold red]value: {argv}")
727	    sc.console.print(f"[bold red]best match: {best_match['args']}")
728	    sc.console.print(f"[bold red]{best_match_score} out of {argc} arguments matched")
729	    sys.exit(1)
730	
731	
732	config_substitution_re = re.compile(r"<\{(.*?)(?<!\\)}")
733	
734	
735	def process_config(data: Any, path="") -> Any:
736	    if isinstance(data, dict):
737	        for key, value in data.items():
738	            new_path = f"{path}.{key}" if path else f"{key}"
739	            data[key] = process_config(value, new_path)
740	    elif isinstance(data, list):
741	        for index, item in enumerate(data):
742	            new_path = f"{path}[{index}]"
743	            data[index] = process_config(item, new_path)
744	    elif isinstance(data, str):
745	        data = re.sub(
746	            config_substitution_re,
747	            lambda m: config_substitution(m.group(1), path),
748	            data,
749	        )
750	    return data
751	
752
```

917	        sc.options.verbose = 3  # force verbose output
918	    elif (sc.options.all and len(sc.options.sites) != 0) or (
919	        not sc.options.all and len(sc.options.sites) == 0
920	    ):
921	        sys.exit("You must specify either at least one site or the --all option.")
922	    if sc.options.verbose:
923	        sc.debug("Arguments:")
924	        pprint(sc.options)
925	        pprint(terminus("self:info"))
926	
927	    # Create a directory named "build" if it doesn't exist:
928	    if not os.path.exists("build"):
929	        os.makedirs("build")
930	
931	    sc.invoke_hooks("setup")
932	
933	    sc.debug(f"Doing post-setup configuration substitutions")
934	    sc.config = process_config(sc.config)
935	    if sc.options.verbose:
936	        sc.debug("Configuration after substitutions:")
937	        pprint(sc.config)
938	
939	    overage_block_size = sc.config["Pantheon"]["overage_block_size"]
940	    overage_block_cost = sc.config["Pantheon"]["overage_block_cost"]
941	
942	    sc.debug(
943	        "[bold magenta]=== Connecting to the [green]pantheon-sitehealth-emails[/green] traffic database:"
944	    )
945	
946	    if sc.config["Database"]["type"] == "sqlite":
947	        traffic_db_conn_str = f"sqlite:///{sc.config['Database']['name']}"
948	        traffic_db_conn_kwargs = {}
949	    elif sc.config["Database"]["type"] == "mysql":
950	        traffic_db_conn_str = (
951	            f"mysql+mysqldb://{sc.config['Database']['user']}:{sc.config['Database']['password']}@"
952	            f"{sc.config['Database']['host']}:{sc.config['Database']['port']}/{sc.config['Database']['name']}"
953	        )
954	        traffic_db_conn_kwargs = {"pool_size": 10, "max_overflow": 20}
955	    else:
956	        sys.exit(f"Unsupported database type: {sc.config['Database']['type']}")
957	
958	    db_engine = db.create_engine(
959	        traffic_db_conn_str,
```

round(0.5) -> 0 (banker's)\n        (5000, 1),       # round(1.0) -> 1\n        (10000, 2),      # round(1.5) -> 2 (banker's rounds the .5 up here)\n        (15000, 2),      # round(2.0) -> 2\n        (20000, 3),      # non-decreasing in overage\n        assert n >= 0\n        prev = n\n\n\n# ── contract_year_end: True only for June 16-29 ──────────────────────────────────────\n@pytest.mark.parametrize(\n    \"date,expected\",\n    [\n        (datetime.date(2026, 6, 16), True),\n        (datetime.date(2026, 6, 29), True),\n        (datetime.date(2026, 6, 22), True),\n        (datetime.date(2026, 6, 15), False),\n        (datetime.date(2026, 6, 30), False),\n        (datetime.date(2026, 5, 20), False),\n        (datetime.date(2026, 7, 20), False),\n        (datetime.date(2026, 12, 25), False),\n    ],\n)\ndef test_contract_year_end(psh, date, expected):\n    assert psh.contract_year_end(date) is expected\n\n\n# ── estimate_month_visits: extrapolate the final partial month ───────────────────────\ndef _dates(*yyyymm):\n    return [datetime.date.fromisoformat(m + \"-15\") for m in yyyymm]\n\n\ndef test_estimate_complete_month_returns_minus_one(psh):\n    # 15 <= last_day < 25 -> (2*extrapolate + previous) / 3  (synthetic last_day; real months\n    # never have <25 days, but the helper is pure and must honor its inputs).\n    vbm = {\"2026-02\": 300, \"2026-03\": 40}\n    extrapolate = 40 * 20 / (10 - 1)\n    assert psh.estimate_month_visits(vbm, _dates(\"2026-02\", \"2026-03\"), 20, 10) == round(\n        (2 * extrapolate + 300) / 3\n    )\n\n\ndef test_estimate_early_month_blends_previous(psh):\n    # {
  "file_path": "/workspace/tests/unit/test_plan_costs.py",
  "content": "\"\"\"Unit tests for plan_costs — the pure cost model extracted from main() (test-suite SPEC\nPart A; the U-M downgrade guardrails / notices remain in main() and are covered by the golden).\n\nplan_costs does no DB I/O: overage-protection state is injected via op_lookup(month) -> record\n| None, so we drive it with SimpleNamespace stand-ins for PantheonOverageProtection rows.\nExpected costs are hand-computed and pinned.\n\"\"\"\nimport datetime\nimport types\n\nimport pytest\n\npytestmark = pytest.mark.unit\n\nBLOCK_SIZE = 10000\nBLOCK_COST = 40.0\nJAN = datetime.date(2025, 1, 1)\n\n\ndef months(start_year_month, n):\n    \"\"\"Return n consecutive 'YYYY-MM' keys starting at start_year_month.\"\"\"\n    y, m = (int(x) for x in start_year_month.split(\"-\"))\n    out = []\n    for _ in range(n):\n        out.append(f\"{y:04d}-{m:02d}\")\n        m += 1\n        if m > 12:\n            m, y = 1, y + 1\n    return out\n\n\ndef vbm(start, n, visits):\n    return {mo: visits for mo in months(start, n)}\n\n\ndef op_none(_month):\n    return None\n\n\ndef op_used(used):\n    return lambda _month: types.SimpleNamespace(used_this_month=used)\n\n\ndef call(psh, plan_info, visits_by_month, *, estimate=-1, op_lookup=op_none, v=None):\n    plan_names = list(plan_info)\n    keys = list(visits_by_month)\n    if v is None:\n        v = [visits_by_month[k] for k in keys]\n    return psh.plan_costs(\n        plan_info,\n        plan_names,\n        visits_by_month,\n        v,\n        estimate,\n        keys[-1],\n        JAN,\n        BLOCK_SIZE,\n        BLOCK_COST,\n        op_lookup,\n    )\n\n\n# ── No overage: cost == base cost; costs_best == max(same, median) ───────────────────\ndef test_no_overage_costs_are_base(psh):\n    plan_info = {\n        \"Basic\": {\"cost\": 500, \"traffic_limit\": 35000},\n        \"Performance Small\": {\"cost\": 1925, \"traffic_limit\": 35000},\n    }\n    cost_same, costs_median, costs_best, median_visitors = call(\n        psh, plan_info, vbm(\"2025-01\", 12, 10000)\n    )\n    assert cost_same == {\"Basic\": 500.0, \"Performance Small\": 1925.0}\n    assert costs_median == {\"Basic\": 500.0, \"Performance Small\": 1925.0}\n    assert median_visitors == 10000\n    # Conservative selection metric.\n    assert costs_best == {p: max(cost_same[p], costs_median[p]) for p in plan_info}\n\n\n# ── Overage with an OP record present but unused -> full overage billed ───────────────\ndef test_overage_no_waiver(psh):\n    plan_info = {\"P\": {\"cost\": 100, \"traffic_limit\": 0}}\n    cost_same, costs_median, costs_best, median_visitors = call(\n        psh, plan_info, vbm(\"2025-01\", 12, 10000), op_lookup=op_used(False)\n    )\n    # 10000 overage -> round((10000+5000)/10000)=2 blocks -> $80/mo * 12 + $100 base.\n    assert cost_same[\"P\"] == 100 + 80 * 12\n    # costs_median uses months_without_op=8 for a non-Basic plan.\n    assert costs_median[\"P\"] == 100 + 2 * BLOCK_COST * 8\n    assert costs_best[\"P\"] == max(cost_same[\"P\"], costs_median[\"P\"])\n\n\n# ── OP used_this_month=True zeroes every month's overage ─────────────────────────────\ndef test_overage_fully_waived_by_used_op(psh):\n    plan_info = {\"P\": {\"cost\": 100, \"traffic_limit\": 0}}\n    cost_same_waived, _, _, _ = call(\n        psh, plan_info, vbm(\"2025-01\", 12, 10000), op_lookup=op_used(True)\n    )\n    cost_same_billed, _, _, _ = call(\n        psh, plan_info, vbm(\"2025-01\", 12, 10000), op_lookup=op_used(False)\n    )\n    assert cost_same_waived[\"P\"] == 100  # base only\n    assert cost_same_waived[\"P\"] < cost_same_billed[\"P\"]\n\n\n# ── Retroactive protection: no OP record, -01 month resets a 4-month waiver window ────\ndef test_retroactive_waiver_window(psh):\n    plan_info = {\"P\": {\"cost\": 100, \"traffic_limit\": 0}}\n    cost_same, _, _, _ = call(\n        psh, plan_info, vbm(\"2025-01\", 12, 10000), op_lookup=op_none\n    )\n    # Jan resets op_remaining=4 -> Jan-Apr waived (4 months), May-Dec billed (8 * $80).\n    assert cost_same[\"P\"] == 100 + 80 * 8\n\n\n# ── estimate > 0 replaces the final month's visits in the cost projection ─────────────\ndef test_estimate_substituted_for_final_month(psh):\n    plan_info = {\"P\": {\"cost\": 0, \"traffic_limit\": 0}}\n    v = vbm(\"2025-01\", 12, 0)  # all months zero...\n    with_estimate, _, _, _ = call(\n        psh, plan_info, dict(v), estimate=100000, op_lookup=op_used(False)\n    )\n    without, _, _, _ = call(psh, plan_info, dict(v), estimate=-1, op_lookup=op_used(False))\n    # 100000 overage on the last month -> round((100000+5000)/10000)=10 blocks -> $400.\n    assert with_estimate[\"P\"] == 400\n    assert without[\"P\"] == 0\n\n\n# ── Fewer than 12 months -> median-fill extrapolation to a full year ─────────────────\ndef test_short_history_extrapolated_to_twelve_months(psh):\n    plan_info = {\"P\": {\"cost\": 100, \"traffic_limit\": 0}}\n    cost_same, _, _, _ = call(\n        psh, plan_info, vbm(\"2025-01\", 6, 10000), op_lookup=op_used(False)\n    )\n    # 6 months at $80 + (12-6) * median([$80]*6) = 480 + 480, plus $100 base.\n    assert cost_same[\"P\"] == 100 + 480 + 480\n\n\n# ── median_visitors reflects v with the estimate swapped into the last slot ───────────\ndef test_median_visitors_uses_estimate(psh):\n    plan_info = {\"P\": {\"cost\": 0, \"traffic_limit\": 10_000_000}}  # no overage anywhere\n    visits_by_month = vbm(\"2025-01\", 5, 1000)\n    v = [1000, 1000, 1000, 1000, 1000]\n    _, _, _, median_visitors = call(\n        psh, plan_info, visits_by_month, estimate=999999, v=v\n    )\n    # v[-1] becomes 999999 before the median -> median of [1000,1000,1000,1000,999999].\n    assert median_visitors == 1000  # middle value unaffected, but no crash and correct pick\n"
}

Matches the first token but the expression is longer than the sub's args -> no full match.\n    reset_sc.substitutions.append(_sub([\"a\"], lambda: \"x\"))\n    with pytest.raises(SystemExit):\n        psh.config_substitution(\"a b\", \"p\")\n\n\ndef test_none_result_exits(psh, reset_sc):\n    reset_sc.substitutions.append(_sub([\"nothing\"], lambda: None))\n    with pytest.raises(SystemExit):\n        psh.config_substitution(\"nothing\", \"p\")\n\n\ndef test_process_config_recurses_dict_list_str(psh, reset_sc):\n    reset_sc.substitutions.append(\n        _sub([\"greet\", \"$who\"], lambda who: f\"HELLO {who}\", [\"$who\"])\n    )\n    data = {\n        \"a\": \"<{ greet x }\",\n        \"b\": [\"<{ greet y }\", 5],\n        \"c\": {\"d\": \"<{ greet z }\"},\n        \"n\": 42,\n    }\n    out = psh.process_config(data)\n    assert out[\"a\"] == \"HELLO x\"\n    assert out[\"b\"] == [\"HELLO y\", 5]\n    assert out[\"c\"][\"d\"] == \"HELLO z\"\n    assert out[\"n\"] == 42\n\n\ndef test_process_config_result_reflects_data_available_at_call_time(psh, reset_sc):\n    # Why main() runs process_config again after the setup hooks: a substitution's return value\n    # reflects the backing data available WHEN it runs.  Two runs, changed data -> changed result.\n    state = {\"v\": \"before\"}\n    reset_sc.substitutions.append(_sub([\"s\"], lambda: state[\"v\"]))\n\n    first = psh.process_config({\"x\": \"<{ s }\"})\n    assert first[\"x\"] == \"before\"\n\n    state[\"v\"] = \"after\"  # e.g. a setup hook populated the data\n    second = psh.process_config({\"x\": \"<{ s }\"})\n    assert second[\"x\"] == \"after\"\n\n\ndef test_plain_strings_are_untouched(psh, reset_sc):\n    out = psh.process_config({\"a\": \"no substitution here\", \"b\": 7})\n    assert out == {\"a\": \"no substitution here\", \"b\": 7}\n"

space:\noverage_blocks monotonicity/non-negativity, and plan_costs never crashing while returning a\nwell-formed, internally consistent result.\n\"\"\"\nimport datetime\n\nimport pytest\nfrom max_value=5_000_000), min_size=5, max_size=13))\ndef test_plan_costs_wellformed_and_consistent(psh, visits):\n    keys = _months(len(visits))\n    visits_by_month = dict(zip(keys, visits))\n == set(PLAN_NAMES)\n    assert median_visitors >= 0\n    for p in PLAN_NAMES:\n        # Costs are the base plan cost plus non-negative overage, so never below base.\n        assert cost_same[p] >= costs_best[p] == max(cost_same[p], costs_median[p])\n"

```
356	def wp(siteenv: str, *args) -> (Any, str):
357	    """
358	    Run a "wp eval" command through Terminus and return the result as JSON.
359	    """
360	    command = ["wp", siteenv, "--", *args, "--format=json"]
361	    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)
362	    try:
363	        result = json.loads(output)
364	    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
365	        result = None
366	        errors += "\n" + output + "\n" + str(e)
367	    return result, errors.strip(), fatal
368	
369	
370	def wp_eval(siteenv: str, *args) -> (str, str):
371	    """
372	    Run a "wp eval" command through Terminus and return the result as a string.
373	    """
374	    command = ["wp", siteenv, "--", "eval", *args]
375	    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)
376	    return output.strip(), errors.strip(), fatal
377	
378	
379	def wp_error(site: str, code: str, message: str, errors: str) -> list[dict]:
380	    html_message = message.replace(site, f"<strong>{site}</strong>")
381	    return [
382	        {
383	            "type": "alert",
384	            "icon": "&#x1F6A8;",  # police car light
385	            "csv": f"{site},wp-error,{code},{json.dumps(errors).replace(',', '\\,')}",
386	            "short": f"fix WP CLI error",
387	            "message": f"""
388	<p>{html_message}
389	<code>wp</code> (WP CLI) returned the following error:</p>
390	<pre>{html.escape(errors)}</pre>
391	""",
392	            "text": f"""
393	{message}
394	"wp" (WP CLI) returned the following error:
395	
396	----- START WP CLI ERROR -----
397	{errors}
398	----- END WP CLI ERROR -----
399	
400	""",
401	        }
402	    ]
403	
404	
405	def fix_drush_output(output: str, errors: str) -> (str, str):
406	    """
407	    Move any error messages at the start of the output from a Drush command to the errors string.
408	    """
409	    if not isinstance(output, str) or output == "":
410	        return output, errors
411	
412	    if output[0] != "{":
413	        lines = output.split("\n")
414	        linenum = 0
415	        while linenum < len(lines):
416	            if lines[linenum] and lines[linenum][0] == "{":
417	                break
418	            linenum += 1
419	        errors = "\n".join(lines[:linenum]) + errors
420	        output = "\n".join(lines[linenum:])
421	
422	    sc.debug("Drush output:\n", output, "\nDrush errors:\n", errors, level=2)
423	
424	    return output, errors
425	
426	
427	def drush(siteenv: str, *args) -> (Any, str):
428	    """
429	    Run a "drush" command through Terminus and return the result as a JSON object.
430	    """
431	    command = ["drush", siteenv, "--", *args, "--format=json"]
432	    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)
433	    output, errors = fix_drush_output(output, errors)
434	    try:
435	        result = json.loads(output)
436	    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
437	        result = None
438	        errors += "\n" + output + "\n" + str(e)
439	    return result, errors.strip(), fatal
440	
441	
442	def drush_php_script(siteenv: str, script: str) -> (Any, str):
443	    """
444	    Run a "drush php:eval" command through Terminus and return the result as a string.
445	    """
446	    command = ["drush", siteenv, "--", "php:script", "--format=json", "-"]
447	    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command, script)
448	    output, errors = fix_drush_output(output, errors)
449	    try:
450	        result = json.loads(output)
451	    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
452	        result = None
453	        errors += "\n" + output + "\n" + str(e)
454	    return result, errors.strip(), fatal
455	
456	
457	def drush_error(site: str, code: str, message: str, errors: str) -> list[dict]:
458	    html_message = message.replace(site, f"<strong>{site}</strong>")
459	    return [
460	        {
461	            "type": "alert",
462	            "icon": "&#x1F6A8;",  # police car light
463	            "csv": f"{site},drush-error,{code},{json.dumps(errors).replace(',', '\\,')}",
464	            "short": f"fix drush error",
465	            "message": f"""
466	<p>{html_message}
467	<code>drush</code> returned the following error:</p>
468	<pre>{html.escape(errors)}</pre>
469	""",
470	            "text": f"""
471	{message}
472	drush returned the following error:
473	
474	----- START DRUSH ERROR -----
